  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_3be01b2d-35db-4aee-84ec-3235dc3315fc'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

              <span id="reviewTextContainer473035968" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3193400326351156035"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400185i/775240._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400185i/775241.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> <i> “This is forever, Maggie. I would follow you to hell if I had to.” His breath tickled my skin. He kissed my temple. “You are all I want for the rest of my life.” </i> </b><br/><br/>Oh. Wow…. *clutches heart* I SO loved this book!!!<br/><br/><b> Maggie and Clay’s story was a deeply touching, heavy and emotional journey of the intensity, strength and beauty of first love coupled with the heart-wrenching hardships and struggles of someone affected by bi polar disorder. </b><br/><br/>This book shows you the light, pulls you into the dark and</span>
  <span id="freeText3193400326351156035" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400185i/775240._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400185i/775241.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <i> “This is forever, Maggie. I would follow you to hell if I had to.” His breath tickled my skin. He kissed my temple. “You are all I want for the rest of my life.” </i> </b><br><br>Oh. Wow…. *clutches heart* I SO loved this book!!!<br><br><b> Maggie and Clay’s story was a deeply touching, heavy and emotional journey of the intensity, strength and beauty of first love coupled with the heart-wrenching hardships and struggles of someone affected by bi polar disorder. </b><br><br>This book shows you the light, pulls you into the dark and then shows you a glimmer of light again.<br><br>I really *felt* for this book. My heart went out to Clay as he struggled with his illness and my heart went out to Maggie as she followed her heart and stood by him no matter what.<br><br><b> The book felt REAL – the journey, the characters, the struggles… Everything that happened was believable, powerful, and very well written and I found myself unable to stop thinking about the story even when I wasn’t reading it. </b><br><br>The prologue hooked me immediately. Having finished the book, I realize how completely it represents it – part beautiful, part despairing, part hopeless, and part desperately and unconditionally in love.<br><br>I loved the writing style!! Like way freaking LOVED it! The story was told from Maggie’s POV and there was just enough humor and sarcasm to keep me almost smiling, but it also had a wonderfully direct, no bull$hit ring to it that made it really easy for me to connect with her. The author perfectly captured that mature yet distinctly older teenage voice – defining that line between teenage and adult.<br><br>The story is about Maggie – a seventeen-year-old girl with a very average, normal, happy-yet-boring life. One day, late for class, she quite literally runs into a guy – Clay. He’s angry, growly and absolutely gorgeous but his attitude throws her off… and yet, she can’t stop thinking about him and seeks him out, determined to become his friend.<br><br>The more time they begin to spend together, the more his moodiness lifts and she begins to see into the inner Clay – the one he doesn’t show the world. He’s fun, jokes around, flirts and is sweet but shy, yet protective…. mercurial. His moods changed constantly and he’d go from happy and light to angry and closed off at the slightest trigger.<br><br>The more he begins to trust her, the more he feels comfortable telling her and when he opens his secrets about his mental health she decides that its not something she’s going to let keep them apart.<br><br>There’s a quiet intensity to the story that builds as an undertone. You know something is off about them but you can’t put your finger on it and the part of you that’s in love with them falling in love with each other just desperately wants to try and dismiss your worries as just something you’re imagining. But… *sigh* they’re not imagined. They’re real. Oh so real. And heart breaking.<br><br>I loved Maggie – like really, truly loved her. She had a straight up, direct, in-your-face, no sugar coating, no bullshit kind of attitude. Throw in a dash of sarcasm and an immensely huge heart and yeah, she was a wonderful heroine who I admired and I never once wanted to throttle! How often does THAT happen??<br><br>Clayton really stole my heart – issues and all. On one hand he was swoony, sweet and had that dash of charm and protectiveness that made my heart flutter and yet, on the other hand his illness made him moody to an extreme, prone to random outbursts and hurtful actions brought about from extreme insecurity.<br><br>Despite all the issues they were working though, Clay and Maggie were truly beautiful together. With every fiber of my being I wanted to find a way for them to be okay.<br><br><i> <b> “I needed Clay as much as he needed me. We existed in this symbiotic relationship where our hearts beat and our lungs breathed only for each other.” </b></i> <br><br>It broke my heart watching Clay break down or have an outburst because you could just tell when it wasn’t ‘him’ – and he was always SO sorry afterward that you just *knew* he meant it.<br><br>He wasn’t just a regular guy, he was one of those swoony, gorgeous Alpha-in-the-making heroes (he’s only 17) and what made it the most heart breaking was that he was a little bit broken. I just wanted to hug him over and over again!! … when he said “I love you, baby” my heart would just MELT!!<br><br><i> <b> “I love you. You are my life.” he placed my hand over his heart. I could feel it beating erratically beneath my palm. “Feel that? It’s yours. For now and always!” </b></i> <br><br><i> “When you’re in a room, Maggie, all I see is you. You make everything better. Clearer. You stop the crazy noise in my head. I can think, hell, I can <b> breathe </b> when we’re together. What you make me feel is the most unbelievable and scary thing I’ve ever felt.“ </i><br><br>He was also such an interesting character because despite having the issues and imbalance, he was very knowledgeable about it. He knew his condition and acknowledged it. It didn’t stop it from affecting him everything time, but it was interesting to see him both so clinically understanding of his condition and at the same time so uncontrollably affected by it. He could explain every single issue he had, he knew and acknowledged every mistake he made, but… he couldn’t stop himself from making them.<br><br>Everything Clay did, wrong or right just broke my heart because, with the way the story is written, you could see exactly what triggered each of his reactions and you could understand them. I mean even though his reactions were over-the-top due to his illness, WHAT he was reacting to was completely understandable which made everything even more painful.<br><br><i> <b> “The struggle is really hard sometimes. And then I meet you. And I feel stuff that I’ve never felt before. Things that I never thought I would be lucky enough to experience. And I feel so out of control in the way I am with you. Like I’m stripped bare and for once someone sees everything inside of me… the good and the really really ugly.” </b></i> <br><br>My heart broke for him – for the hell he lived in back home, for his struggles, for his efforts to be better. Even without his disorder, the fucked up relationship he had with his parents would have driven ANYONE to extremes. Heck even reading some of the things he had to go through in his home life made ME want to loose it.<br><br>Its weird to say this but given what Maggie and Clay were going though, I’d actually call them very functional as a couple. I don’t think they could have handled their situation better. Every thing that went wrong for them was heavily influenced by external forces beyond their control but, between the two of them, they were really doing their best to figure things out. But they were in an impossible situation, facing impossible odds for which there was no magic solution and no quick fix.<br><br><i> <b> “And if he went into the dark again, this time I would be there to find him – to follow him. Because I thought, perhaps quite immeasurable that my love could help him. Maybe our love could even do more than just help – maybe it could heal him. Fix him. Fix everything.” </b></i> <br><br>The book really builds after about 70%. And in the final 20%, I was pretty much just reading with this ohGodohGodohGod feeling as things went from bad to worse and I just wanted it to work out SO badly.<br><br>By 94% I was crying. A lot….<br><br> <br><br>I know a lot of you have been asking <b> whether there’s a cliffhanger </b> so I’m going to try and answer that here:<br><br>The way I’d describe it is that it ended at a good stopping point (like, not in the middle of a scene or anything) but it was definitely only half their story – there is a lot more to tell. You definitely do know that its the RIGHT place for the characters to be at this time AND the next book, <i> Light In The Shadows </i> is already out so you don't have to wait to finish their story!<br><br>This book has easily made it onto my favorites pile and the author’s writing style was brilliant. I’d definitely recommend this book.<br><br>5 stars.<br><br> <br>CASTING (see above and below):<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400186i/775242._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400186i/775243._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400186i/775244.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400186i/775245.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400186ra/775246.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

<div id="review_470330747" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/470330747" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/470330747?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=freaking-cliffhanger">freaking-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=young-adult-fiction">young-adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer470330747" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer780242728958374096"><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You ran into my life, this beautiful, amazing girl who changed everything." ~ Clay</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399784i/774007._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"And maybe what we had, for those few blissful months, had truly been beautiful. Crazy beautiful. Or maybe just crazy."</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/><b>WOW. Just...WOW.</b> After finishing this story I honestly didn't know what to do with my emotions. And actually I didn't know what to do with them while I was reading it either. I felt like I was on an emotional roller coaster that only went up, up, up and that was bound to come down </span>
  <span id="freeText780242728958374096" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You ran into my life, this beautiful, amazing girl who changed everything." ~ Clay</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399784i/774007._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"And maybe what we had, for those few blissful months, had truly been beautiful. Crazy beautiful. Or maybe just crazy."</b>
</i><br><br><br><b>WOW. Just...WOW.</b> After finishing this story I honestly didn't know what to do with my emotions. And actually I didn't know what to do with them while I was reading it either. I felt like I was on an emotional roller coaster that only went up, up, up and that was bound to come down in the most harsh and hurtful way, and it did (sort of). I haven't felt that emotional and "on edge" while reading a book since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13312527.The_Opportunist__Love_Me_With_Lies___1_" title="The Opportunist (Love Me With Lies, #1) by Tarryn Fisher" rel="nofollow noopener">The Opportunist</a>, but I absolutely LOVED every minute of it!!!! <br><br><br><b>Find You in the Dark</b> is the story about <b>Maggie May Young</b> and <b>Clayton Reed</b>, it's a story about how these two young people fall in love, how they struggle with all the harshness and trouble life has to offer, and how they never, not once fall <i>out</i> of love. But sometimes, love itself is not enough...<br><br><br><b>Clay --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399784i/774008._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Maggie --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399784i/774009._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Goodness is your virtue. Quiet beauty your weapon."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The seventeen year old Maggie Young is living the perfect teenage life where everything is normal. She has good grades, great friend and nice, loving parents. But then, one day, she meets Clay. At first, they don't get along too well; Clay is very distant, a little rude and it's obvious he doesn't like to allow people close into his life. But Maggie is determined to change that. She's drawn to him in an unexplainable way and Clay himself, can't seem to stay away from her either. He's never met anyone who truly cared about <i>him</i> and who showed him what it feels like to be loved.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I was this sad and lonely creature before you came along. And then, just being with you, knowing you love me, has transformed me. My entire life has become this metamorphosis into something beautiful, something happy. I told you before that you've freed me. You've reminded me of what it means to <i>believe</i> and <i>hope</i>." ~ Clay</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Clay isn't always an easy person to be around, he's often surrounded by dark thoughts...because of his condition he has a lot of mood swings. There are a lot of ups and downs in their relationship but when things were good. They were fantastic.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"And if he went into the dark again, this time I would be there to find him - to follow him." ~ Maggie</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399784ra/774010.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their love really is crazy. And beautiful. Crazy Beautiful. It's intense and all consuming for both of them and I constantly felt like things were bound to end badly...<br><br></p><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I knew his love was an intense, hungry thing. I worried for a moment, as I fell asleep, that his love would eat me alive." ~ Maggie</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Their love was like a ticking time bomb; where I was desperately hoping that I would be wrong and that the bomb wouldn't explode, but like so many other things in life, you can't always get what you're hoping for... Clay and Maggie were such easy to love characters. They both had their good and their bad qualities (especially Clay) but even when they did mess things up, they were easy to forgive because they managed to capture my heart and all I wanted for them was to get the happy ending they so desperately deserved.<br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399784ra/774011.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>When I asked him as to why he only drew the butterflies, he kissed me softly on the mouth. "Because you make me feel free."<br><br>"You're my butterfly, baby."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399784ra/774012.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I needed Clay as much as he needed me. We existed in this symbiotic relationship where our hearts beat and our lungs breathed only for each other."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399784ra/774013.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br>The last few chapters leading up to, what I would call, one of the most heartbreaking endings EVER, were SO emotional. Really, things kept getting worse and worse to the point where I wanted to literally step inside the book and intervene, but on the other hand, I also KNEW things were headed in that direction, the entire time I was reading. So, to say that it surprised me wouldn't be true but I would say that it did make me cry, a lot. And for that I'm glad I waited to read this book until the sequel was released because I just NEED to find out how the story continues and therefore I'll be reading the next one right away!!!<br><br><i>Find You in the Dark</i> is an amazing, beautiful, unforgettable, heart wrenching story and and absolute <b>MUST READ</b>. It's a story that will stay with me forever and I already know this series will be from now on residing on my <b>all time favorites</b> shelf. <br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399784ra/774014.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><i>
  <b>"I love you so much. Sometimes it hurts."<br><br>"I don't want it to hurt, Clay. Our love should make you feel wonderful."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><br><b>♥ 5 CRAZY BEAUTIFUL STARS. ♥</b><br><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="780242728958374096" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_707840128" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/707840128" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7453310-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1533143862p2/7453310.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/707840128?book_show_action=true">Aug 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/7453310-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7453310-sarah?shelf=bad-romance">bad-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer707840128" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12855601626426813166">DID I READ THE WRONG BOOK?!?<br/><br/>What in the HELL was that. This is just fucking scary that these girls are rating it five stars.<br/><br/>Not only are there editing issues, but the plot was all over the fucking place.<br/><br/>Where in this book did you find a love story? Because in the book that I READ, I was rooting for a girl called Maggie May to get the hell out of some twisted, mind-fuck, mentally abusive relationship. Which sadly for me looks like it wont happen. This is just awful.<br/><br/>Is it love to be embarrassed in</span>
  <span id="freeText12855601626426813166" style="display:none">DID I READ THE WRONG BOOK?!?<br /><br />What in the HELL was that. This is just fucking scary that these girls are rating it five stars.<br /><br />Not only are there editing issues, but the plot was all over the fucking place.<br /><br />Where in this book did you find a love story? Because in the book that I READ, I was rooting for a girl called Maggie May to get the hell out of some twisted, mind-fuck, mentally abusive relationship. Which sadly for me looks like it wont happen. This is just awful.<br /><br />Is it love to be embarrassed in front of your classmates because your boyfriends crazy possessive?<br />Is it love when youre that nasty couple dry humping(my imagination here) in the cafeteria, so much so that the principal comes over to tell you to cut the shit?<br />Is it love when youre purposely distancing yourself from the relationships youve had since you were a baby because your boyfriends jealous and feels left out?<br />FINALLY, FOR FUCKS SAKE, IS IT LOVE WHEN YOUR BOYFRIEND INSTIGATES AND PUSHES YOU TO HAVE SEX WITH HIM IN A PUBLIC PARK ON A COLD ASS FUCKING BENCH ON A FALL NIGHT? If that turns you on, honey, then youll like this book. I felt dirty and ready to get this book over with since 30%. Ms. Walters youve wasted 6 hours of my life. The time it took me to make the money to buy your shitty book to the time it took me to read it.<br />Heed this review!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12855601626426813166" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_460841922" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/460841922" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/460841922?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2018-ya-challenge">2018-ya-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2018-audio">2018-audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer460841922" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9696660719891228"><b>5+ stars!</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>And if he went into the dark again, this time I would be there to find him- to follow him. Because I thought, perhaps quite immaturely, that my love could help him. Maybe our love could do more than just help- Maybe it could heal him. Fix him. Fix everything.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>This is a story of first loves, intense and passionate. A story of two people, so in love, they thought it was all they needed. If they had each other, everything would be okay. Their love was crazy and it was beautiful.</span>
  <span id="freeText9696660719891228" style="display:none"><b>5+ stars!</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>And if he went into the dark again, this time I would be there to find him- to follow him. Because I thought, perhaps quite immaturely, that my love could help him. Maybe our love could do more than just help- Maybe it could heal him. Fix him. Fix everything.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />This is a story of first loves, intense and passionate. A story of two people, so in love, they thought it was all they needed. If they had each other, everything would be okay. Their love was crazy and it was beautiful. It bordered on being obsessive at times. This is a story of two people who become completely dependent on each other for their happiness. This is the story of Clayton and Maggie. <br /><br />Maggie was an ordinary high school senior. She was close with her parents and her two best friends, Rachel and Daniel. She was involved in sports, did well in school. She led a fairly average, yet boring life. That is until she met Clayton. Clay was a new student who transferred from a school in Florida. He seemed standoffish in the beginning to everyone. He was quiet and mysterious. Maggie literally ran into him. She knew there was something special about Clay. Despite his withdrawn personality, they became friends. Maggie quickly realized Clay had some issues. He could have terrible mood swings, and sometimes just seemed off. Other times, he could be wonderful. Their friendship grew and they developed strong feelings for one another. They fell in love. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Have there ever been two people who loved each other as much as we did? I couldn't put it into words the way we felt about each other. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Maggie was exceptionally devoted to Clay. There were many times she should have walked away from him, but she stayed. Her parents and friends tried to be supportive, but grew to be concerned for her and Clay's relationship. Their love for each other was heart warming and heart breaking. They were addicted to each other.<br /><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>We existed in this symbolic relationship where our hearts beat and our lungs breathed only for each other. Was all first love this intense?</b>
  </blockquote>
</i><br />Clay- I adored Clay. If you know anyone who suffers from mental illness, you know how difficult it can be for that person. His parents make it harder than it already is. Mags is everything to Clay. Without her, I'm not sure what would have happened to him. Its scary to think about. He truly loves her, but he can become manic, get possessive and extremely jealous- which is very taxing on their relationship. She can be really helpful to Clay, but also enables him some.<br /><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"When you're in a room, Maggie, all I see is you. You make everything better. Clearer. You stop the crazy noise in my head. I can think, hell, breathe when we're together."</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br />I really rooted for Clay and Mags to make it. Even though their relationship was dysfunctional, it was beautiful as well. Clay's letter to Mags at the end of the book had me in tears. The author did an amazing job with this story and the characters. The end gave me hope for Clay and Maggie. I cannot wait for the sequel! No one deserves a happy ending more than these two. I'm so glad this is not the end of their story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9696660719891228" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer462231313" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10229070596702960475">I can’t even deal with what I’m feeling right now. I finished this morning but have not been able to write a review because of the pain I feel right now. <br/><br/>I purchased this book three years ago and like most of my books it got buried in a pile on my kindle. <br/><br/>I didn’t read the blurb I just plunged into the book. The title, <b>Find Me in the Dark, </b> should have clued me in on what I was getting into… mental illness. There’s a stigma with that illness unlike the more acceptable health issues that deal wit</span>
  <span id="freeText10229070596702960475" style="display:none">I can’t even deal with what I’m feeling right now. I finished this morning but have not been able to write a review because of the pain I feel right now. <br><br>I purchased this book three years ago and like most of my books it got buried in a pile on my kindle. <br><br>I didn’t read the blurb I just plunged into the book. The title, <b>Find Me in the Dark, </b> should have clued me in on what I was getting into… mental illness. There’s a stigma with that illness unlike the more acceptable health issues that deal with one’s physical being. Talking about someone’s diabetes is okay <b>contrary</b> to talking about someone's depression. In our society there’s shame with being mentally “weak.” <br><br>I’ve read Ms. Walter’s other series, <i> Reclaiming the Sand</i>, and I realize that she likes to make me feel uncomfortable while reading about her characters’ stories. When I got to the end of this one I was struggling to finish it because one of my closest friends did a similar thing that happens in the end of the book. That scene alone triggered a lot of memories for me and has thrown me into a funk. <br><br>Talking about our personal experiences can be very therapeutic and yet right now I feel vulnerable because this book hit home for me. Everyone has book triggers that make some stories next to impossible, for them, to read because of personal experiences. The story becomes too real and painful. My personal experience with my friend has made reading and writing this review very painful. So I'm going to leave you with: <br><b> <i>You Found Me</i> by The Fray </b><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://youtu.be/jFg_8u87zT0">http://youtu.be/jFg_8u87zT0</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421292354i/13354520._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(In loving memory of my friend, Bill. I will forever miss and love you)<br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16081754.Find_You_in_the_Dark__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_" title="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1359627731s/16081754.jpg" alt="Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) by A. Meredith Walters" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17155039.Light_in_the_Shadows__Find_You_in_the_Dark___2_" title="Light in the Shadows (Find You in the Dark, #2) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1359612980s/17155039.jpg" alt="Light in the Shadows (Find You in the Dark, #2) by A. Meredith Walters" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Continuing story<br><br><i>Novellas:</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16163857.Cloud_Walking__Find_You_in_the_Dark___1_5_" title="Cloud Walking (Find You in the Dark, #1.5) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1357550690s/16163857.jpg" alt="Cloud Walking (Find You in the Dark, #1.5) by A. Meredith Walters" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18106519.Warmth_in_Ice__Find_You_in_the_Dark___2_5_" title="Warmth in Ice (Find You in the Dark, #2.5) by A. Meredith Walters" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1382103673s/18106519.jpg" alt="Warmth in Ice (Find You in the Dark, #2.5) by A. Meredith Walters" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Teenagers sometimes do reckless things and what these two did was too bad.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401268i/778622.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"You told me I was your forever.<br>Now prove it."</b><br><br>From this point of the book things are getting way too crazy.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401268ra/778623.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401268i/778624.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401268ra/778625.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I loved so much this book.The way they meet each other is ordinary but the rest of the story will definitely captivate you.This is not an easy read , though. Clay's <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[mood changes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> are happening all the time and sometimes it is scary.Maggie is a very strong girl.Dealing with these issues is very difficult and she handled it pretty well except from the end.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I dont agree with the run away part. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>"If you are feeling lost , well , I'll have to find you."~Maggie<br><br>"Your love saved me."~Clay</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380659i/737615.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer463715596" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4484770346552704106"><b>
  <i>4.5 Stars<br/><br/>”And maybe what we had, for those few blissful months, had truly been beautiful. Crazy beautiful. Or maybe just crazy.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398803i/771024._SY540_.jpg' width='350' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Thank you A. Meredith Walters for giving life to Clayton Reed!<br/> <br/><i>Find You in the Dark</i> is a true to life depiction of a young adult suffering from mental illness. We experienced his highs and lows, manic episodes, his anger and his desperation to feel normal through the point of view of his girlfriend Maggie.<br/><br/>I too love someone who suffers some of the same problems as C</span>
  <span id="freeText4484770346552704106" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>4.5 Stars<br><br>”And maybe what we had, for those few blissful months, had truly been beautiful. Crazy beautiful. Or maybe just crazy.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398803i/771024._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Thank you A. Meredith Walters for giving life to Clayton Reed!<br> <br><i>Find You in the Dark</i> is a true to life depiction of a young adult suffering from mental illness. We experienced his highs and lows, manic episodes, his anger and his desperation to feel normal through the point of view of his girlfriend Maggie.<br><br>I too love someone who suffers some of the same problems as Clayton. Mental Illness affects not only the diagnosed but their family and friends as well. <br><br>As a reader it broke my heart to read how Clayton’s peers picked up on his social awkwardness and labeled him different from the get go. Maggie fell for Clayton and saw past his illness and took the time to be his friend. <br><br>Clayton and Maggie fall in love and their relationship followed the array of highs and lows much like Clayton’s mental state.<br><br>Clayton’s love for Maggie was so intense but kudos to Maggie she stood by him where others may have walked away. Although it terrified her she never let him down or alone in the dark.<br><br><b>
  <i>"This is forever, Maggie. I would follow you to hell if I had to." His breath tickled my skin. He kissed my temple. "You are all I want for the rest of my life." <br><br>"But I knew his love was an intense, hungry thing. I worried for a moment, as I fell asleep, that his love would eat me alive."</i>
</b><br><br>Things begin to spiral out of control. Maggie’s love gave him something to hold onto to but is that enough? <br><br>I have high hopes that Clayton can become the man he wants to be. I’m looking forward to the sequel!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1571268364i/28305279.jpg" width="301" height="301" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“You ran into my life, this beautiful, amazing girl who changed everything. I finally saw what my world could be. What being normal and happy could look like."</i>
</b><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8611843384645493078"><blockquote>
  <b>“Goodness is your virtue. Quiet beauty your weapon.”</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399449ra/772984.gif' width='450' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Find You in the Dark</i> is a beautifully written story of a young women looking to feel something other than normal and a young man looking to feel just normal. <br/><br/>This heartbreakingly real and gut-wrenching portrayal of a young man suffering crippling mental illness and his journey of survival through the love and salvation of a young women, totally gutted me; I fell completely and deeply in pain and in love with Clay and Maggie. <br/><br/>Their story was</span>
  <span id="freeText8611843384645493078" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>“Goodness is your virtue. Quiet beauty your weapon.”</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399449ra/772984.gif" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Find You in the Dark</i> is a beautifully written story of a young women looking to feel something other than normal and a young man looking to feel just normal. <br><br>This heartbreakingly real and gut-wrenching portrayal of a young man suffering crippling mental illness and his journey of survival through the love and salvation of a young women, totally gutted me; I fell completely and deeply in pain and in love with Clay and Maggie. <br><br>Their story was honest and felt so real, and it breaks my heart to know that many young people are suffering through this type of pain. <br><br>The author created a story based on her own experience working ten years as a counselor for at risk teens and children at a Domestic Violence/Sexual Assault program and then later a program for children with severe emotional and mental health issues.<br><br> <br><b>"When I asked him as to why he only drew the butterflies he had kissed me softly on the mouth. Because you make me feel free.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399449i/772985._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>“You ran into my life, this beautiful, amazing girl who changed everything.   <b>"I realize my love for you crippled both of us. But your love saved me."-Clay</b>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_438145318" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/438145318" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/438145318?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer438145318" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer53255334731502723"><b>5 FANTASTIC CLAYTON AND MAGGIE STARS</b><br/><br/><b>Phenomenal!!! ABSOLUTELY PHENOMENAL!!!</b> This book is an emotional, touching story, that takes us on a journey as we discover the hardships of someone suffering from a serious mental illness and how that illness can affect every facet of their lives as well as those they love. Mental health does not discriminate, affecting millions of people throughout the world. It’s a scary thing and something that is heart wrenching to read about. <br/><br/>I went into this book blind </span>
  <span id="freeText53255334731502723" style="display:none"><b>5 FANTASTIC CLAYTON AND MAGGIE STARS</b><br><br><b>Phenomenal!!! ABSOLUTELY PHENOMENAL!!!</b> This book is an emotional, touching story, that takes us on a journey as we discover the hardships of someone suffering from a serious mental illness and how that illness can affect every facet of their lives as well as those they love. Mental health does not discriminate, affecting millions of people throughout the world. It’s a scary thing and something that is heart wrenching to read about. <br><br>I went into this book blind without reading the synopsis or any reviews. I chose it based on the amazing cover alone. HOLY CRAP was I blown away. Not only is this a story about mental illness but also of first love; a strong and addictive first love. It was powerful!! Clayton’s struggle with his mental disorder was truly sad, leaving me feeling broken and intensely wounded for him and his girlfriend Maggie, who experienced his destructive behavior first hand. There was such realness to this book that it took my breath away leaving me completely entranced and feeling that the author’s characters came alive leaving a lasting imprint in my life. <br><br><b>
  <i>“The struggle is really hard sometimes. And then I meet you. And I feel stuff that I’ve never felt before. Things that I never thought I would be lucky enough to experience. And I feel so out of control in the way I am with you. Like I’m stripped bare and for once someone sees everything inside of me… the good and the really really ugly.” ~~ Clayton </i>
</b><br><br>Maggie Young is in her last year of high school and is ready for her life start. She’s sick of the everyday normal and wants to experience something different, that’s not the mundane day to day. Rushing to class and not looking were she’s going Maggie runs over a very annoyed Clayton Reed. Not exactly impressed with Clayton’s attitude their first meeting leaves a bad taste in Maggie’s mouth. Their second encounter takes place in the lunch room and goes equally poorly leaving Maggie stumped wanting to know who the grumpy, very sexy new boy really is. There’s a connection to Clay that Maggie just can’t ignore as she sets out to find out everything she can by getting close to him. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Hot damn. Cue the violins and happy cartoon bunnies. I was in the middle of a Disney moment. Because this guy was gorgeous. And we were standing so close to each other. If he hadn't been holding onto a barely contained rage directed at yours truly, it could have almost been construed as romantic.” ~~ Maggie </i>
</b><br><br>Maggie is a go-getter, a girl after my own heart. She has a mouth on her that made me laugh out loud. I loved how strong and courageous she was. Her feelings for Clay were palpable and I truly understood her need to be there and support Clay even when things were not looking good. It ripped me apart to read Maggie's slow break down and see how the relationship took its toll on her. Being with someone that's so unhealthy can cripple even the sanest person. I'm a firm believer that we do not chose who we love that love chooses us and it broke my heart that Maggie couldn't get what she needed from Clay because he was so incredibly unstable, he didn't have it to give to her.<br><br>Clay....oh Clay :( This boy! Let me say you will fall head over heels in love with Clay. That nurturing instinct takes over when you read this book and all you want to do is save this boy. Help him in some way. Hold him. I don't even know but I wanted to save Clay from himself. This subject is hard, really, really hard. Clay has a dynamic personality with so much potential but his issues are immense. <br><br>Clay and Maggie fall in love. It's such a dysfunctional, unhealthy but passionate and strong type of love. I remember what it was like as a teenager to feel a love that's so strong it's crippling and becomes the center of your universe. Maggie and Clay have that and you become enraptured in their feelings for each other and the constant yo-yo state of their relationship. Their love story is an angsty book lovers dream, it's so full of gut wrenching pain. I guarantee you will cry!!!!! I cried like a baby.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I needed Clay as much as he needed me. We existed in this symbiotic relationship where our hearts beat and our lungs breathed only for each other.” ~~ Maggie </i>
</b><br><br>I highly recommend this book. It made it to my favorite's shelf without a doubt. It was an incredible moving, thought provoking book. I am so invested in these characters. The ending left me screaming, needing and craving more. I can't wait to get my hands on book 2. I think this author is brilliant and her writing was absolutely wonderful. I loved it. &lt;3<br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Clay and Mags &lt;3</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394919i/760526.jpg" height="255" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><i>
  <b>“What is it?" I asked breathlessly. <br>"I love you so much. Sometimes it hurts."<br>"I don't want it to hurt, Clay. Our love should make you feel wonderful.” </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394919i/760527.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>“Love is the absence of judgment.” ― Dalai Lama </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394919i/760528.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="53255334731502723" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_474118709" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/474118709" />
    <a title="Annie Brewer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer"><img alt="Annie Brewer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442496062p2/5315988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/474118709?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie Brewer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie Brewer" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer">Annie Brewer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=emotionally-devastating">emotionally-devastating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=not-for-everyone">not-for-everyone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=tearjerker">tearjerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=nook-books">nook-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=teen-sex">teen-sex</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=tbr-kindle">tbr-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=hard-core">hard-core</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer474118709" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11157547124987099137">Wow, I'm in absolute tears and depression right now. This was such a hard book to read. I cried through most of it. I need to get my emotions together to write my review. But after reading the sneak peek for the sequel which is in Clay's POV, I am more than positive that there is light at the end of the tunnel, somewhere. But this is NOT an HEA, so if you're looking for that in this book, don't look further. I need the sequel now!!! My heart hurts so bad for these characters. <br/><br/>Full review to come</span>
  <span id="freeText11157547124987099137" style="display:none">Wow, I'm in absolute tears and depression right now. This was such a hard book to read. I cried through most of it. I need to get my emotions together to write my review. But after reading the sneak peek for the sequel which is in Clay's POV, I am more than positive that there is light at the end of the tunnel, somewhere. But this is NOT an HEA, so if you're looking for that in this book, don't look further. I need the sequel now!!! My heart hurts so bad for these characters. <br><br>Full review to come...<br><br>Okay, I am not sure how to start this. This book still weighs heavy on my mind since I finished at 4 am. But I will start out by giving this author kudos, for addressing such a heavy issue and doing it tragically beautiful. I don't know how she did it, but this is definitely a book that will stay with me for a long time. I've known people in my life who suffered from bi-polar disorder and personality disorder. These are NOT easy issues to cover. But somehow, I was thrown into this darkness that I could not climb out of, much like Clay Reed. So, with that said...Good job A Meredith Walters. It proves me to be even more of a masochist, but I am okay with that. It's books like these that make me love reading so much more. And if that makes me sick, then so fucking be it. <br><br>So we have Maggie Young, a seventeen year old who is in her senior year of high school. She's a sweet and caring person. She loves her family and her two best friends, Rachel and Daniel and would do anything for them. Her life is anything but fun. She does the same things everyday and is not at all spontaneous. She starts to wish there was something more to life than this monotony she lives through. Don't we all??<br><br>That is...til she runs into Clay Reed, literally runs into him in the school parking lot. He's the new student who moved from Florida. He's dark, mysterious and oh so good looking. Everyone tries to bully him, especially the popular jackass Paul who makes a scene at lunch one day. Yelling at Clay, calling him a pussy and breaking his MP3 player. But Clay does nothing but keep his head down and his gaze anywhere but on Paul. To Maggie, it's very disconcerting that he would let such a prick humiliate him in front of everyone so she intervenes. He's not happy about the save, letting Maggie know it was not her business. What is he a Damsel in Distress? No guy wants a girl to "save" them from public humliation-it's embarrassing and takes their "man card" away. What....ever. <br><br>Clay:<br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/clay.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400347i/775625.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After all the cold shoulders and hissing that Clay does, Maggie has had enough. She's intrigued by his secretive side and wants to know more about him so she makes it a mission to butt into his life. And she won't back down. Much to Clay's dismay, he finally lets her in..a little at a time. He shows her a little bit of living and she finally gets to see what spontaneous is like. She stops hanging out with her friends to spend as much time with Clay as possible. Their friendship grows and soon becomes something more, they fall in love. It also becomes destructive and fast. Because there seems to be a wall between them, something that Clay is still hiding from her. When she finally learns his family history and of his sickness, she does everything in her power to save him. But is love really enough?<br><br>Maggie and Clay:<br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/clayandmaggie.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400347i/775626.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Ahhhhh, this book. It broke me to pieces. I was on pins and needles. Constantly biting my nails in fear, frustration, pain and anger. Clay suffers from mental health issues. His parents were never the loving type, in fact his parents are probably a big reason he's so fucked up and I HATE THEM!!! They are inconsiderate, self-centered, evil people. They always blamed him for his issues and called him every bad name in the book, making him feel like an embarrassment. How the hell can you call yourself a parent when you're anything but...evil sons of bitches. Yes, excuse the cursing but his mother made me want to throw my nook at my wall and then sob. I hated how she acted toward Maggie and blamed her for everything that's wrong with him. Fuck you. Ugh. That woman got under my skin like no other.<br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/iwillburnyougif.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400347ra/775627.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Seriously, I know this is a hard book to read but I couldn't stop-and didn't want to. I've dealt with this kind of stuff and its not pretty. But the author really did a good job of dragging me into the pits of hell with Clay and all I wanted to do was.....<br><br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/sadgif2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380365501ra/717597.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It was so hard to read what he was going through. I cried, I sobbed and I wanted to help Maggie too. She was so helpless, thinking that her love would save him-them. That all you need is love. But sometimes, even love isn't enough. Sometimes the darkness sucks you under so quickly, you can't breathe...<br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/loveisnotenough.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400347ra/775628.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Just when I thought things were going to be okay....<br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/sadgif3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364509ra/716212.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I was a mess. I couldn't breathe. I cried so much. I felt Maggie's pain, her helplessness, her fear...everything. I loved Clay. He was a broken and very sick boy. I wanted him to have a happy ending. But sometimes even happy endings are impossible.<br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/sadgif1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400347i/775629.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don't know if this book is for everyone, but those that can handle such monumental issues will like this. Those that are masochists like me....read it. I want to discuss this book with others. I want opinions...<br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/sadgif.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400347ra/775630.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If you choose to read this, just know there is a sequel...and its from his POV and I can't effing wait. I want it....NOW!!! I'm dying here....I want more. I love them. Maggie and Clay. I want them to have a happy ending. Dammit to hell. This is me at the last page....<br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/media/sadgif5.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400347ra/775631.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I loved Maggie for being one of the only people that really loved Clay. The only one that wanted to help him-even though she may in some way enabled his tendencies. But what did she know? She got in too deep and couldn't get out, because she loved him enough to try and help him. Unlike his parents who did nothing but make him feel worthless and want to end his life. There were many things that happened in this book that made you question whether it was right or wrong. Maggie wanted to live a perfect normal life with her amazing boyfriend, and sometimes he was amazing. But in an instant, his moods went off the handle and he was a complete dick. How do you justify your relationship with that person? That's not love, yet she would not give up on him. It broke my heart. I feared for his life and for hers as well. Gah, this is hard. I can clearly visualize everything that happened. I loved Rachel and Daniel too. They were good friends and even though they didn't understand what was happening, they were always there for Maggie. <br><br>All in all, the writing was great! The story, obviously a hard pill to swallow, the characters were memorable and the end....well the end will kill you. Just have tissues handy. And then when you read Clay's POV in the back-a sneak peek at the sequel, you'll feel a sense of hope for the future. Maybe a light....go to the light. Ahhhh I want...I want that book NOW NOW NOWWW! Please don't make me wait too long. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11157547124987099137" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9138738-georgia"><img alt="Georgia ♥ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1377186210p2/9138738.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/454269005?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Georgia ♥ " href="/user/show/9138738-georgia">Georgia ♥ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=the-sound-of-my-heart-breaking">the-sound-of-my-heart-breaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=another-freaking-cliffhanger">another-freaking-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=favourite-cause-it-is-unique">favourite-cause-it-is-unique</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=in-love-with">in-love-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=sobbing-mess">sobbing-mess</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer454269005" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15622045840837034437"><b>★★★★★ Darkness & Freedom ★★★★★</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>♪♫ Hello darkness, my old friend,<br/>I've come to talk with you again♪♫ </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397390ra/766763.gif' width='400' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There are many kinds of darkness and many kinds of bonds. The worst are the absence of light in a soul and the restrictions we alone inflict upon us. We are our own worst enemies and we abuse ourselves. It takes more than guts to break what holds you back. To see the fault in you. To ask for help. And stop saying I'm sorry.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>Sometimes “sorry” is not enough. Sometimes you actually have to change</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText15622045840837034437" style="display:none"><b>★★★★★ Darkness &amp; Freedom ★★★★★</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>♪♫ Hello darkness, my old friend,<br>I've come to talk with you again♪♫ </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397390ra/766763.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are many kinds of darkness and many kinds of bonds. The worst are the absence of light in a soul and the restrictions we alone inflict upon us. We are our own worst enemies and we abuse ourselves. It takes more than guts to break what holds you back. To see the fault in you. To ask for help. And stop saying I'm sorry.<br><br><i>
  <b>Sometimes “sorry” is not enough. Sometimes you actually have to change.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397390i/766764.png" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Maggie Young</b> is a normal 17-year old girl. An average student with friends, family and dreams that every teenager has. Her world will change forever when it collides with <b>Clayton "Clay" Reed</b>. And they fall irrevocably in love...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397390i/766765.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Clay is anything but normal. A dead 17-years old, deep in his soul. Damaged, alone, despaired. Beyond repair? Maggie will fight heaven and hell to prove that there is nothing irredeemable in him. To love him forever, as he will always love her. Possessively and insanely. Beautiful.<br><br><i>
  <b>“When you're in a room, Maggie, all I see is you. You make everything better. Clearer. You stop the crazy noise in my head. I can think, hell, I can breathe when we're together What you make me feel is the most unbelievable and scary thing I've ever felt.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379799794i/659692.jpg" width="400" height="298" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Sometimes, though, love is just not enough and you have to set the other free and wait, praying that he/she will come back. Stronger and larger than life.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397390i/766766.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I can't stretch enough the sheer amount of feelings and beauty I went through reading this story. How much drawn I was to these kids. I rooted for them, I cried and crumbled along them. And I despaired at the injustice they had to face...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397390ra/766767.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book deals with a really serious and sensitive matter, in the most respectful way. With tenderness and care, treating it like the fragile wings of a butterfly that Clay is enjoying to draw, because he yearns to fly, leaving his failing mind behind and be finally free.<br><br><i>
  <b>“Just wanted to know how it felt to fly.”<br><br>“Because you make me feel free.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/440163.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>By the end I was left a sobbing mess trying and failing to mend the piece of my broken heart, just like the shattered dreams of Maggie and Clay's...<br><br><i>
  <b>"You deserve so much more than me. You always have. I hope you do find what you deserve one day.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397390ra/766768.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>WARNING:</i>Do NOT start this book without having the next already loaded in you reading device!</b><br><br>But I urge you... Read this story and find an once-in-a-lifetime kind of love.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397390i/766769._SX540_.gif" width="500" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>This review can be found on my blog: <a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">infinity-of-time.blogspot.com</a> also known as... </i>
</b><br><a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.gr/2013/04/find-you-in-dark-find-you-in-dark-1-by_20.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380363317i/714576.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/475283071?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Fathima" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Fathima" href="/user/show/5799807-fathima">Fathima</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>
