        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer475283071" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4990889830217297196"><b>
  <i>“I can't do this by myself. I don't know what to do, or what to say. I can't help you if you don't want to help yourself.” I said matter of factly.  <br/>Clay looked at me for a second, then crossed the room toward me. “That's where you're wrong. You save me every single day. You are the one thing that makes me happy. You are the only thing I need.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>OMHYGOD !!!!!!<br/><br/>WHAT IN THE WORLD !!!!! <br/><br/>AHHHH , MY HEARD HURTS ... AND MY HEART .. DONT EVEN TALK ABOUT IT ! IT'S SHREDDED .... NOTHING ... ALL GONE ...</b></span>
  <span id="freeText4990889830217297196" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“I can't do this by myself. I don't know what to do, or what to say. I can't help you if you don't want to help yourself.” I said matter of factly.  <br>Clay looked at me for a second, then crossed the room toward me. “That's where you're wrong. You save me every single day. You are the one thing that makes me happy. You are the only thing I need.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>OMHYGOD !!!!!!<br><br>WHAT IN THE WORLD !!!!! <br><br>AHHHH , MY HEARD HURTS ... AND MY HEART .. DONT EVEN TALK ABOUT IT ! IT'S SHREDDED .... NOTHING ... ALL GONE ... <br><br>IF NOT FOR THAT LITTLE TEASER IN THE END FROM THE SEQUEL .... I'D BE SOOOOO DOING THIS :<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=THROWINGAFIT.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400524ra/776356.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>BUT STILL , TRUTH BE TOLD ... I CANT HELP MY EMOTIONS , THEY ARE ALL OVER THE PLACE ....<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=Crying.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400524ra/776357.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>I CANT THINK STRAIGHT .... REVIEW TO FOLLOW TOMORROW OR DAY AFTER OR WHENEVER .... </b><br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=sadgif.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/477676.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> Edit : 16/12/2012 </b><br><br>Honest to everything sane and insane , I'm still speechless over what to write as a review for this book . Why you ask ?? Because I feel that words can never justify the intensity of emotions that manage to barrel their way across the pages and hit the reader with force . I'm not saying that its going to be like that for everyone who reads this book . But for me , this was closer to hitting home . And reading it was like revisiting those dark recesses of the mind that have been completely locked away . But irrespective of whether you've heard , seen , or experienced something similar or not , you will definitely relate to certain things mentioned or described here . That I guarantee !<br><br>This is not exactly a review ... I mean I'm trying to write one but it may not end up being one .. Please bear with me . Its like I just wanna talk and stuff ...<br><br><i> Cue * <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=7FO8zUseF2k" rel="nofollow noopener"> Sleeping with ghosts - Placebo </a> </i> I was soo freaking happy when this is played in the book , its one of my fav albums by Placebo and this song is like <b> WOW !!! </b> <br><br>Find you in the Dark is the story of Maggie May Young . Maggie is a normal girl , with normal parents , normal friends , normal life ... you know typical seventeen year old stuff . For her , Love is what her parents have for each other . Not the typical high school dating scenario . Simple life , no boyfriend hassle what-so-ever.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Let's start over.  Hello, my name is Maggie Young.  Seventeen year old self- confessed choc-o-holic and over all fabulous human being.  Pleased to meet you.”</i>
</b><br><br>But things change , right ? So did Maggie's life . The day Clayton Reed bumped into her . <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=Clay2.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400524i/776358.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Clay is not like the other guys Maggie has ever know . He is someone entirely too different . He doesn't talk to anyone , keeps to himself and seems lost . Maggie is intrigued . She wants to know him .. And Maggie is persistent . Her persistence finally pays off ...<br><br><b>
  <i>Clayton slowly reached out and clasped my hand in his.  His handshake was firm and made those obnoxious butterflies in my stomach take flight at the feel of his warm skin against mine.  His smile was wide and genuine, making his brown eyes sparkle.  “Clayton Reed, though you can call me Clay.  Seventeen year old senior and unabashed misanthrope.”</i>
</b><br><br>Which then leads to Maggie and Clay becoming friends . <br><br>But Clay has issues ... Very dark , deep rooted issues that can destroy anything and everything in its path . <br><br>He says he's fine ... but he isn't .. <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=376472_357169577685910_635981685_n.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400524i/776359.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maggie and Clay's relationship takes a turn and starts changing into more than ' just friends' ... <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=butterflies.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400524ra/776360.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But then Maggie finds out what Clay is all about .. Will she stick around or will she run away ? Will Clay change or will it too late for Maggie to turn her back and walk away ??? <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=k-Love--sense--raia--bw--trend_large.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400524i/776361._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is definitely one of the 'most emotional' stories that I've read this year . My emotions would jump from extreme happiness to extreme sadness .. Many a times I found myself shouting and asking<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=whay-is-happening.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400524ra/776362.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maggie and Clay ... My god I cant even begin to describe what I was feeling seeing them go back and forth all the freakin time ! Strictly speaking , other than Clay's parents , I couldn't blame any of the characters for the parts they were playing in this story . If I had a best friend who was dating a guy like Clay , I would have totally blasted her ass off and asked her not to bother with him anything . Or If I would have been a parent who saw their daughter dating him , I would be like , ' No way young lady , he is trouble !!! Stay away from him . ' But just like Maggie I would have stuck to Clay no matter what . Do you know why ?? Because its usually loneliness , being treated differently , being ignored or shunned away that is the major cause for people with mental instability . I've had friends who are exactly like Clay , and I know why they are who and what they are .. I've seen them suffer . Seen them try to make a place for themselves in this so called 'society' ... But I've seen them being rejected , being treated like outcasts , being told that they aren't good enough ! I've seen battle their demons and losing . And then what happens ? They just become a shell , hollow from the inside . No positive feelings or emotions , only rage . <br><br>Maggie and Clay's love also faces similar problems in the story . Maggie's decision to stick with Clay only damages her relationship with others ..<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=followyouinthedark.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400524i/776363.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=Downfall.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400524ra/776364.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But for Clay , Maggie is all he wants . Her love is all he wants ..<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=somuchbetter.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400524ra/776365.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And Maggie gives him exactly that .. She loves him without a doubt . Even though he hurt her at times , she forgives him and tries to make things alright for him .. with him .<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=takemyhandsandrun.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400524ra/776366.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“What is it?” I asked breathlessly, never stopping the perfect rhythmic movements with him.  Clay smiled, a truly gorgeous smile.  “I just love you so much.  Sometimes it hurts.”  “I don't want it to hurt, Clay.  Our love should make you feel wonderful.”</i>
</b><br><br>But is that enough ?? It's not . A relationship , that is constantly clouded by doubts , uncertainty and despair is never a successful one is it ? <br><br>Personally , I feel that Clay's parents are to ultimately be blamed for all his troubles . <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=angry.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400524ra/776367.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>All they cared about was their social status . "What would people think if they found out our soon was an addict with major mental issues ?? " seemed to be the only thing that really bothered them ! And his mom , lord , I've never met a mom like her ..... EVER !!! I despised her from the core of my being !! Such people calling themselves parents has to be the biggest joke that life can play on someone ! <br><br>The ending ! <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=Crawlanddie.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400524ra/776368.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Totally broke my heart , whatever was left of it .. all done with ! Reading that letter was like reading a life sentence note ! I was bawling like an idiot , going all ' NO NO NO , this is not it ... please dont let it be that ... oh god why .... ' .. Talk about a soul shattering cliffhanger ... <br><br><b>This book is a must read ! A.Meredith Walters takes a very important teen issue that has plagued many and spins a beautiful story of love and friendship . A story that is bound to make you smile one moment and cry the next . </b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4990889830217297196" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_477630116" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/477630116" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/477630116?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=emotional-reads">emotional-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=angst-filled-reads">angst-filled-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=bad-boy">bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=got-it-in-paperback">got-it-in-paperback</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer477630116" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7391633815298706188"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390507460i/8234391._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400871i/777338._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Nooooo!!! No No No!!! Oh my goodness! I don't <i>do</i> stories without a happy ever after. This book has torn me to shreds! I was so emotionally invested and I feel like I'd had the world ripped out from under me at 2.30am, when I finished the book, last night.<br/><br/>Mean mean mean author!!<br/><br/>However, it has to be said, <i>Find You in the Dark</i> was absolutely superb writing. The book was totally gripping. I loved the characters so much. Maggie was brilliantly funny, strong and down to earth. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Hot damn. Cue t</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText7391633815298706188" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390507460i/8234391._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400871i/777338._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nooooo!!! No No No!!! Oh my goodness! I don't <i>do</i> stories without a happy ever after. This book has torn me to shreds! I was so emotionally invested and I feel like I'd had the world ripped out from under me at 2.30am, when I finished the book, last night.<br><br>Mean mean mean author!!<br><br>However, it has to be said, <i>Find You in the Dark</i> was absolutely superb writing. The book was totally gripping. I loved the characters so much. Maggie was brilliantly funny, strong and down to earth. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Hot damn. Cue the violins and happy cartoon bunnies, I was in the middle of a Disney moment. Because this guy was gorgeous.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>It was fascinating to see the inevitable change in her personality due to her relationship with Clay. You could feel her slipping deeper and deeper away from the happy-go-lucky family girl she once was with no control over what was happening.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Why are you interested in me?" He asked quietly. Hmm. How to answer that one? I didn't want to tell him that I thought he was the most gorgeous creature I had ever seen and wanted to have his babies. That might be a little much.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Clay was a completely heart-wrenching, lost soul. I wanted him to be saved so badly. I totally got Maggie's motivation to do the things she did. Who wouldn't, for Clay? The author made me crave his happy side, just as Maggie did.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I wanted to feel what it was like to kiss you for the first time without being sucked into a medicated fog."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>His love for Maggie was terrifyingly deep. He <i>needed</i> her, in the strongest sense of the word. It was unhealthy, yet beautiful and true, in equal measures. <br><br>This book delved into such harrowing, life altering issues that it was difficult not to get sucked in. And the ending shattered me. Be aware that this book does <i>not</i> give you a happily-ever-after! I can't bare the thought of Clay having to live a life without Maggie. Surely a person, with issues such as Clay's, can regulate their conditions enough to live a semi-ordinary life? Does he not deserve love too? Argh, I can't bare it!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"The struggle is really hard sometimes. And then I meet you. And I feel stuff that I've never felt before. Things that I never thought I would be lucky enough to experience. And I feel so out of control in the way I am with you. Like I'm stripped bare and for once someone sees everything inside of me... the good and the really really ugly."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And the letter. O-M-actual-G! I bawled my eyes out at the letter. I wanted to scream and throw my kindle and stamp my feet. I was gutted. This is <i>not</i> how I wanted it to end. However, I just can't give it less than four stars, because I just adore Clay and Maggie and am still holding out hope...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I needed Clay as much as he needed me. We existed in this symbiotic relationship where our hearts beat and our lungs breathed only for each other.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>There is obviously another book. I can only hope that we get our HEA in that, otherwise I am going to have a full blown tantrum and shit <i>will</i> go down! Pleeeeeease A. Meredith Walters, give Maggie her Clay back.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400871i/777339._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743250626754/?fref=ts">http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743...</a></span>

<div id="review_515575505" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/515575505" />
    <a title="Monisha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13001527-monisha"><img alt="Monisha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433436407p2/13001527.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/515575505?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Monisha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Monisha" href="/user/show/13001527-monisha">Monisha</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13001527-monisha?shelf=aww-melting-inside">aww-melting-inside</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer515575505" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15763250800789644322"><b>OH.MY.GOD <br/>What an absolutely stunning book! <br/>SO MUCH EMOTION!</b><br/><br/><br/>So we have Maggie Young:<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406535i/793267._SY540_.jpg' width='300' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>A seventeen year old who is in her senior year of high school.<br/>Her life is anything but fun. <br/>She is bored of her perfect little life and when a new student with less than the perfect attitude appears at her perfect school she is drawn to him....<br/><br/><b>CLAY.</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406535i/793268.jpg' width='300' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The boy in a very shattered world who can’t break enough things.<br/><br/>And he’s beautiful and he works at a bookstore and he’s a desert storm in a jar.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406535i/793269.jpg' width='300' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Dark hair and onyx ey</span>
  <span id="freeText15763250800789644322" style="display:none"><b>OH.MY.GOD <br>What an absolutely stunning book! <br>SO MUCH EMOTION!</b><br><br><br>So we have Maggie Young:<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406535i/793267._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>A seventeen year old who is in her senior year of high school.<br>Her life is anything but fun. <br>She is bored of her perfect little life and when a new student with less than the perfect attitude appears at her perfect school she is drawn to him....<br><br><b>CLAY.</b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406535i/793268.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The boy in a very shattered world who can’t break enough things.<br><br>And he’s beautiful and he works at a bookstore and he’s a desert storm in a jar.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406535i/793269.jpg" width="300" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Dark hair and onyx eyes, with lashes for days.<br><br>That’s the very volatile/mercurial/tumultuous Clayton Reed for you.<br><br>He’s the boy with a war in his mind and his thoughts and actions are falling like casualties.<br><br><br><br><b>"Hot damn. Cue the violins and happy cartoon bunnies, I was in the middle of a Disney moment. Because this guy was gorgeous. And we were standing so close to each other."</b><br><br><br><br>Intrigued by him, she claws her way in Clay's world. <br><br>And she won't back down. Much to Clay's dismay, he finally lets her in....a little at a time. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406535ra/793270.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><br><b> "Why are you interested in me?" He asked quietly.<br>Hmm. How to answer that one? I didn't want to tell him that I thought he was the most gorgeous creature I had ever seen and wanted to have his babies.<br>That might be a little much.</b><br><br><br>He shows her a little bit of living and she finally gets to see what spontaneous is like. <br>Their friendship grows and soon becomes something more, they fall in love.<br><br><span>[image error]</span> <br><br><br> <br><b>When I asked him as to why he only drew the butterflies he had kissed me softly on the mouth.<br>“Because you make me feel free.”</b> ~ Clay <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406535ra/793272.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>It also becomes destructive and FAST!!!<br>Because there seems to be a wall between them, something that Clay is still hiding from her. <br>When she finally learns his family history and of his sickness, she does everything in her power to save him. <br><i>But is love really enough?</i><br><br> <br>Clay's mood swings and irrational jealousy start to affect Maggie's personality. <br>Maggie herself thinks she can help Clay. <br>Clay thinks all he needs is Maggie's love.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406535ra/793273.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>This leads to a highly dysfunctional, all consuming, co-dependent relationship.</i><br><br><br><b>"But I knew his love was an intense, hungry thing. I worried for a moment, as I fell asleep, that his love would eat me alive."</b><br><br><br><br>Clay was a completely heart-wrenching, lost soul. <br>I wanted him to be saved so badly. <br>I totally got Maggie's motivation to do the things she did. <br>Who wouldn't, for Clay? <br>The author made me crave his happy side, just as Maggie did.<br><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/589140.gif" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>"I wanted to feel what it was like to kiss you for the first time without being sucked into a medicated fog."</b><br>Oh. Wow…. *clutches heart*<br><br><br><br>His love for Maggie was terrifyingly deep.<br>He needed her, in the strongest sense of the word.<br><i>It was unhealthy, yet beautiful and true, in equal measures.</i><br><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406535i/793274.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>This book shows you the light, pulls you into the dark and then shows you a glimmer of light again.<br><br><b>
  <u>MY THOUGHTS:</u>
</b><br><br><br>I really *felt* for this book.<br><br><br>Oh my goodness! I don't do stories without a happy ever after. This book has torn me to shreds! I was so emotionally invested and I feel like I'd had the world ripped out from under me at 2.30am, when I finished the book, last night.<br><br>By the end I was left a sobbing mess trying and failing to mend the piece of my broken heart, just like the shattered dreams of Maggie and Clay's...<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406535ra/793275.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"You deserve so much more than me. You always have. I hope you do find what you deserve one day. "</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406535ra/793276.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was literally on the edge of my chair with a blanket pulled over my head for the better part of my day today!! I couldn't read fast enough to see what was gonna happen.....<br><br>I think I'll be pulling an all nighter to read how the story continues!<br>Fingers crossed that everything that they have suffered wasn’t for nothing!!!<br><br></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer474588391" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5903016936857012499">4 Emotional stars!!<br/><br/>This is the story of Maggie.. A fun loving girl whose life changes as she literally runs into a boy...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400419i/775902._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>“Hot damn. Cue the violins and happy cartoon bunnies. I was in the middle of a Disney moment. Because this guy was gorgeous. And we were standing so close to each other. If he hadn't been holding onto a barely contained rage directed at yours truly, it could have almost been construed as romantic.” </b><br/><br/>Meet Clay...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400419i/775903._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>From the moment Maggie meets Clay she is drawn to him like a moth t</span>
  <span id="freeText5903016936857012499" style="display:none">4 Emotional stars!!<br><br>This is the story of Maggie.. A fun loving girl whose life changes as she literally runs into a boy...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400419i/775902._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>“Hot damn. Cue the violins and happy cartoon bunnies. I was in the middle of a Disney moment. Because this guy was gorgeous. And we were standing so close to each other. If he hadn't been holding onto a barely contained rage directed at yours truly, it could have almost been construed as romantic.” </b><br><br>Meet Clay...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400419i/775903._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From the moment Maggie meets Clay she is drawn to him like a moth to a fire... He is everything she thought she never wanted and she is everything he thought he could never have...<br><br>Maggie makes it her mission at befriend Clay and Clay keeps to himself... Afraid to let anyone in... Until Maggie...<br><br>They become friends and then those feelings develop into more... <br><br><b>“Why are you interested in me?” He asked quietly. Hmm. How to answer that one? I didn’t want to tell him that I thought he was the most gorgeous creature I had ever seen and wanted to have his babies. That might be a little much.” </b><br><br>Then Maggie learns about Clays mood crazy mood swings... The source of these behaviors... Clay has a mental illness disorder... We join Maggie in her emotional rollercoaster relationship with Clay..<br><br>When It's good with Clay... It's really good...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400419i/775904._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But when it's bad it's really bad... Clay's erratic behavior... The way he deals with the pain... Maggie wants to save him.. But can she really save him from himself?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400419i/775905.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“The struggle is really hard sometimes. And then I meet you. And I feel stuff that I’ve never felt before. Things that I never thought I would be lucky enough to experience. And I feel so out of control in the way I am with you. Like I’m stripped bare and for once someone sees everything inside of me… the good and the really really ugly"</b><br><br>Then Maggie finds out Clay stopped taking his medication.. It's like every time there is an excuse.. When you love someone, you tend to look past the excuses and errors... And look for what you want to see..<br><br><b>“I wanted to feel what it was like to kiss you for the first time without being sucked into a medicated fog.” </b><br><br><b>“What is it?" I asked breathlessly. <br>"I love you so much. Sometimes it hurts."<br>"I don't want it to hurt, Clay. Our love should make you feel wonderful" </b><br><br>Clays mental health deteriorates slowly and still Maggie loves him sooo much she stands by him... Thinking she can save him... <br><br><b>“I needed Clay as much as he needed me. We existed in this symbiotic relationship where our hearts beat and our lungs breathed only for each other.” </b><br><br>Maggie soon finds out her love isn't enough to save him... He needed to be saved from himself....from hurting himself...<br><br><br><b>“I have learned that sometimes "sorry" is not enough. Sometimes you actually have to change.” </b><br><br>We learn about selfless love... That's what Maggie had... She loves him with the the emotional baggage that he had and then some...<br><br>But sometimes you need to let go... She needed to love what was good for her.. And Clay wasn't good for her... We go through all the heart breaking emotions with Maggie in an incredibly written book...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400419i/775906._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending broke my heart.. Where Clay let her to, to be happy...<br><br><b>“Just know that you are and always will be my world. You found me in the dark and saved me from myself.” </b><br><br>I cannot wait for the next book.. And I hope Maggie and Clay will find their way back to each other..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400419i/775907.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400419i/775908._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9112734511638162856"> <b><i>The sea’s evaporating<br/>Though it comes as no surprise<br/>These clouds we’re seeing<br/>They’re explosions in the sky<br/>It seems it’s written<br/>But we can’t read between the lines</i></b><br/><br/>

<br/><br/>
  <i> Maggie </i>

  <span id="freeText9112734511638162856" style="display:none"> <b><i>The sea’s evaporating<br>Though it comes as no surprise<br>These clouds we’re seeing<br>They’re explosions in the sky<br>It seems it’s written<br>But we can’t read between the lines</i></b><br><br>
  <b> -:- FIVE FORGET-TO-FEED-THE-KIDS STARS! -:- </b>
<br><br>
  <i> Maggie </i>
<br><br>On paper, I’m sure Maggie would look to be your typical, life-symmetrical, <i>normal</i> girl. <br><br>She has very normal hair. A normal face. A normal life with two best friends. She runs cross-country, her parents are still together and very much in love, and she has a 3.5 GPA. (and if anyone so much as <b>thinks</b> to throw their “spoiler” card at me for stating this… Don’t. )<br><br>I mean we all have met this girl in high-school, right? She’s the girl you sit behind in Physics class so you can casually “stretch” behind her during the test you kind of forgot to study for. She’s the girl who, let’s face it, probably made her own pom-poms for Friday’s pep-rally. She uses her blinker when she’s parking in her senior spot, and she’s never late for class. Et cetera. Et cetera…<br><br>The thing is… Maggie Young isn’t normal. She’s a city of a girl. This girl can swear in a way that would make sailors jealous, but she’s riddled with morals and ethics. She’s a structured silhouette of a person, and she’s a fighter. Basically, this girl would be THE Hufflepuff at Hogwarts. <br><br>She stands up to villains.<br><br>And sometimes… she stands up <i> for</i> them.<br><br>
  <i> Clay </i>
<br><br>The boy in a very shattered world who can’t break enough things.<br><br>And he’s beautiful and he works at a bookstore and he’s a desert storm in a jar.<br><br>Dark hair and onyx eyes, with lashes for days. <br><br>That’s the very volatile/mercurial/tumultuous Clayton Reed for you. He’s the boy with a war in his mind and his thoughts and actions are falling like casualties.<br><br>
  <i>Thence, the twain shall meet…</i>
<br><br>
  <b>“Hey!” I yelled as I collided with the very solid body. I dropped my phone, the back popping off and the battery skittering across the concrete. The guy dropped the papers he was holding and they scattered at his feet.<br><br>“What the hell?” The guy growled, stooping to pick up the items he had dropped in our bodily fender bender.<br><br>Hot damn. Cue the violins and happy cartoon bunnies, I was in the middle of a Disney moment. Because this guy was gorgeous. And we were standing so close to each other. If he hadn’t been holding onto a barely contained rage directed at yours truly, it could have almost been construed as romantic.</b>
<br><br>And so it begins.<br><br>
  <a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/LELOVEBLOGSTORIESSUBMISSIONSADVICEPHOTOSKISSESSOFAIRYTALEITMAKESPEOPLESICKYOUAREMYQUEENKINGMARTYNAGALLA_zps2201418a1.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <span>[image error]</span>
  </a>
<br><br>
  <i>Obsession<br>Lust<br>Destruction<br>Infatuation<br>Doubt<br>Addiction<br>Passion<br>Desperation</i>
<br><br>The very fractured Clayton Reed has splinters in his soul and razors in his veins. <br><br>And Maggie loves him.<br><br>These two ribbons of characters become entwined. One is addicted the other, while one is infatuated. <br><br>And it’s a <i> very</i> windy day.<br><br>
  <b> His fingers clenched mine so tightly it was cutting off the circulation. </b>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/508868669?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer508868669" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7270362247868379390">Is there some unwritten rule about this genre that I don't know?<br/><br/><a href='http://s1284.beta.photobucket.com/user/rahime2008/media/done_zpsa258f8e6-1_zpsdf2e6492.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Like many times before, here we have a nice, caring, ordinary girl who meets a mysterious, irresistible, sexy new guy at school with skeletons in his closet, and it's all wrapped up in a high school/friends/parents drama. Sure, it evolves into something more interesting later on, but why put off a reader at the very beginning with same old, same old?<br/><br/><a href='http://s1284.beta.photobucket.com/user/rahime2008/media/Pain/cute_zps29877ff8.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br/><br/>I lost count how many times Clay and Maggie where going back an</span>
  <span id="freeText7270362247868379390" style="display:none">Is there some unwritten rule about this genre that I don't know?<br><br><a href="http://s1284.beta.photobucket.com/user/rahime2008/media/done_zpsa258f8e6-1_zpsdf2e6492.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405519i/790060.jpg" alt="done_zpsa258f8e6 photo done_zpsa258f8e6-1_zpsdf2e6492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Like many times before, here we have a nice, caring, ordinary girl who meets a mysterious, irresistible, sexy new guy at school with skeletons in his closet, and it's all wrapped up in a high school/friends/parents drama. Sure, it evolves into something more interesting later on, but why put off a reader at the very beginning with same old, same old?<br><br><a href="http://s1284.beta.photobucket.com/user/rahime2008/media/Pain/cute_zps29877ff8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>I lost count how many times Clay and Maggie where going back and forth. Him, from loving her madly, to being irrationally jealous and finally pushing her away. Her from having natural doubts about his behaviour, to also being jealous and ending up throwing herself carelessly into a dangerous relationship. I know Maggie is 17, but age is not a factor whether someone should have a common sense or not. <br><br>The constant extreme feelings between the two should have stirred some emotion in me, unfortunately I remained quite distant to the whole story. I just didn't feel it until the very end, the hotel room scene <br><br><a href="http://s1284.beta.photobucket.com/user/rahime2008/media/ww_zps070ce235.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405519ra/790062.gif" alt=" photo ww_zps070ce235.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Suddenly it was all there! The drama, the pain, betrayal, hurt, desperation - all there! And just like that I found myself quite emotional...<br><br><a href="http://s1284.beta.photobucket.com/user/rahime2008/media/Pain/cr3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>A little too late if I think about it now, but it definitely earned an extra star. I just wish that spark happened earlier. It shows that both the story and author have a great potential.<br><br>I have mixed feelings about Find You in the Dark. It didn't grab me at the beginning as I would have liked it to, it was interesting enough for me to carry on reading. I was a bit tired and frustrated in the middle and it totally blew my socks off in the end. I'd recommend it for New Adult/Contemporary fans, though I'm definitely having a break from this genre. I need something fresh, new and exciting...<br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1740661341127777551">Yep, I am in the minority here. Read all the 5 star reviews. Read all the hype about it and jumped on the bandwagon, as usual. The writing was good. The main characters were good but it just dragged on and on for too long.... yes the last 20% was very compelling and heartbreaking but the rest of the book just did not do it for me.   <span id="freeText1740661341127777551" style="display:none">Yep, I am in the minority here. Read all the 5 star reviews. Read all the hype about it and jumped on the bandwagon, as usual. The writing was good. The main characters were good but it just dragged on and on for too long.... yes the last 20% was very compelling and heartbreaking but the rest of the book just did not do it for me. Maybe I am a bit old and jaded to be reading about 17 year old High School students. Will I read the next one? Probably, cos I got sucked into the hype and had already downloaded it before I started this one. I know the subject matter is a tough one. Know families who have been touched by depression and suicide - it is not easy. But overall, just did not do it for me.</span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/515618962?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=sob-fest">sob-fest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-faves-book-1">series-faves-book-1</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer515618962" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16294247628591816029"><b>OMG! What an absolutely stunning book! SO MUCH EMOTION! </b><br/><br/>I feel like this is a book in two parts. The first part is boy meets girl, and all is swoony and gorgeous, and I was completely swept up in the romantic bliss. The second part is a much darker, more emotional read that ripped my heart out in places, and left me crying at the unfairness of it all. <br/><br/>Our heroine is Maggie. And OMG, I absolutely LOVE her! 17 years old, she’s honest, open-minded, sarcastic, and oh so witty. Her inner monologue is</span>
  <span id="freeText16294247628591816029" style="display:none"><b>OMG! What an absolutely stunning book! SO MUCH EMOTION! </b><br><br>I feel like this is a book in two parts. The first part is boy meets girl, and all is swoony and gorgeous, and I was completely swept up in the romantic bliss. The second part is a much darker, more emotional read that ripped my heart out in places, and left me crying at the unfairness of it all. <br><br>Our heroine is Maggie. And OMG, I absolutely LOVE her! 17 years old, she’s honest, open-minded, sarcastic, and oh so witty. Her inner monologue is hilarious. And she constantly speaks her mind, so her dialogue and banter is absolutely sensational! She’s your ‘average’ girl, has two best friends that she has grown up with, loving and supportive parents and no past traumas or issues of any kind. If anything, she’s a little bored of her life and the ‘normal-ness’ of it all. <br><br>And then along comes Clay. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406542i/793311.jpg" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From the very beginning when they literally run into each other, there is a something about Clay that captures Maggie’s attention<br><br><i>“There was something about Clayton Reed that seemed to broadcast vulnerability. The hunch to his shoulders, the refusal to look at anyone. It was as if he didn’t want anyone to see him and that made me want to do just that.” </i><br><br>She is instantly smitten and, being the bold, tenacious girl that she is, needs to know more about him. So she starts to pester him, hanging around, asking personal questions, wanting to get to know him and become friends… or preferably more.<br><br><i>“Why are you interested in me?” He asked quietly. Hmm. How to answer that one? I didn’t want to tell him that I thought he was the most gorgeous creature I had ever seen and wanted to have his babies. That might be a little much.”</i><br><br>Clay and Maggie start hanging out, and form a strong friendship – with some serious chemistry! Clay clearly has some issues, with erratic behaviour and massive mood swings, and Maggie digs deep to try to get him to talk to her, but it isn’t until she witnesses his behaviour at its most extreme that he drops the mother of all bombshells on her and reveals that he is suffering from serious mental illness. Although she is shocked by his revelation, Maggie doesn’t care, and after learning his awful backstory, and all about his hateful parents and neglectful childhood, she vows to be the one to stand by him and support him no matter what - thinking that maybe if she loves him enough, it might just fix him. There are a few bumps along the way, but their friendship soon develops into beautiful and oh-so-swoony, teenage first love. <br><br><i>“You ran into my life, this beautiful, amazing girl who changed everything. I finally saw what my world could be. What being normal and happy could look like. You’ve given me everything I never thought I could have!” </i><br><br>Their love for each other is very deep, and they pretty much exist in their own little bubble, with Clay clinging to Maggie as the one good thing in his life. And, brushing aside concern from her friends about Clay’s behaviour, and her parents’ concern about her total preoccupation with him, Maggie is determined to protect the boy that has become her whole world. <br><br><i>“They had no idea what Clay went through every day. How hard it was for him to hold it together. They didn’t see how beautiful and perfect we were together. They just didn’t get it.” </i><br><br>Clay still battles his illness, and Maggie continues to try to help him - overlooking his mood swings, being there for him, and forgiving him when he treats her badly. And as the book progresses, an undercurrent of sadness and dread starts to form, for as much as they love each other, you know that the happy time can’t last, and it’s all going to fall apart in a horrible, devastating mess. <br><br><i> “I felt like I was trying to hold on to a block of ice as it slowly melted through my fingers. I couldn’t keep hold of the happiness I felt in those moments when things were good. Because the bad loomed not far away, just waiting to wipe everything else away.”</i><br><br>I love, love, love these characters! Maggie and Clay are both absolutely amazing. Clay is such a broken soul. He is desperate for happiness, to have a normal life with the girl that he loves so passionately, but his illness is a constant factor. <br><br><i>“The struggle is really hard sometimes. And then I meet you. And I feel stuff that I’ve never felt before. Things that I never thought I would be lucky enough to experience. And I feel so out of control in the way I am with you. Like I’m stripped bare and for once someone sees everything inside of me… the good and the really, really ugly.”</i><br><br>With his violent mood swings, he lashes out at Maggie, and my heart broke for him as he tried so hard to apologise and make it up to her, and try to be a better person for her. He does everything he possibly can to grab onto her with both hands and never let her go. <br><br><i>“This is forever, Maggie. I would follow you into hell if I had to … You are all I want for the rest of my life.”</i><br><br>Maggie has a huge heart, and would do anything for her “<i>beautiful boy”</i>. She is so committed to him, doing everything she can to help him and support him. But I also loved that she was smart enough to realise that things weren’t quite right. <br><br><i>“I got that he loved me. But was this a love I could deal with? Was this love going to tear me apart?”</i><br><br><i>“His vulnerability broke my heart. How could needing me this much be good for him?”</i><br><br>She battled with the need to be there for Clay and the need to protect herself, and I absolutely loved and admired her for the strength that she showed in doing what she thought was best. <br><br>And then there are Maggie’s best friends, Rachel and Daniel. Together they formed an amazing trio, and I loved the closeness that they shared. They were 100% there for Maggie, and fiercely protective of her, as you would expect best friends to be. Their side story was an unexpected treat, and I am looking forward to reading more about them. <br><br>Maggie and Clay’s story is one emotionally wild ride. The ups and downs in their relationship are gut wrenching, and I was in tears a number of times. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Watching Clay slowly fall apart, and seeing Maggie slowly break down as she comes to realise that she is unable to help him, is devastating! And that letter at the end! OMG!!! Total freaking sob-fest! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This is a beautifully written book. The story, all from Maggie’s POV, is a difficult one to tell, but Walters does it with understanding and incredibly compassionate detail. My heart broke for both Clay and Maggie and all that they went through. And whether I agreed with what they were doing or not, I thought their actions were exactly right for the characters. And the ending, although a bit of a cliffhanger, was absolutely perfect for where the story needed to go. <br><br>I absolutely loved it, and can’t wait to continue on with the next book. <br><br><i> “I realised that despite the hangups, despite the crazy drama he created, I would love him always. Clay was mine just as surely as I was his. My life and his were inexplicably intertwined and there was no denying the intense connection we shared.”</i><br><br>5 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16294247628591816029" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_583669536" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/583669536" />
    <a title="Kristalia " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5705623-kristalia"><img alt="Kristalia " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1535637983p2/5705623.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/583669536?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristalia " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristalia " href="/user/show/5705623-kristalia">Kristalia </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kristalia  by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=wishlist_series">wishlist_series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=favorite-couple">favorite-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=cut-my-heart-out">cut-my-heart-out</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=humans-should-die-here-painfully">humans-should-die-here-painfully</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=it-s-so-hot-in-here">it-s-so-hot-in-here</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=made-me-smile-or-laugh">made-me-smile-or-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5705623-kristalia?shelf=age-new-adult">age-new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer583669536" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13634554913226165642"><b>Final rating: 5/5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> And if he went into the dark again, this time I would be there to find him – to follow him. Because I thought, perhaps quite immaturely, that my love could help him. Maybe our love could do even more than just help – maybe it could heal him. Fix him. Fix everything. </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I need to recover from reading this book. I was gripped from the start and held there, weeping and crying and wanting to strangle someone until it mercifully let me go. This book deals with some se</span>
  <span id="freeText13634554913226165642" style="display:none"><b>Final rating: 5/5 stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> And if he went into the dark again, this time I would be there to find him – to follow him. Because I thought, perhaps quite immaturely, that my love could help him. Maybe our love could do even more than just help – maybe it could heal him. Fix him. Fix everything. </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I need to recover from reading this book. I was gripped from the start and held there, weeping and crying and wanting to strangle someone until it mercifully let me go. This book deals with some serious issues a human being can have, and can handle as well... It can be devastating, but it can be beautiful as well - if you can survive it. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><br>“I was this sad and lonely creature before you came along. And then, just being with you,knowing you love me, has transformed me. My entire life has become this metamorphosis into something beautiful, something happy. I told you before that you've freed me. You've reminded me of what it means to believe and hope.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>It also shows the strength in people, the courage to battle with the unknown, to show that there is always a bright side to everything and that it can always win the dark...But is it really the same when you come face to face with it? <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “I wish we could stay here. You know in our own little bubble.” I said mournfully as Clay placed small, shiver inducing kisses on the underside of my jaw. <br> “We'll just have to move the bubble back to Davidson is all.” Clay said confidently. “But bubbles have a nasty way of popping.” I was being really gloomy, but I couldn't help it. Nothing good ever lasted. <br> “Then we'll just make a new bubble.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>CHARACTERS</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Maggie:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “You are everything. To me you're the world.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>First i need to say one thing: congratulations on such bravery and courage. Many would have fled given the opportunity, or stayed away...but did she give up? NEVER! She wanted to know more about Clay, she wanted to understand the mystery that he emitted...she just wanted to know <i> more</i>. The one thing that i hated about her was the fact that she sometimes pried too much and forced conversations, not to mention her killing curiosity. But, she is one of the rare people who gave everything to <i> help</i>....<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Clay:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “I just wanted to be normal. For once, I wanted to feel normal. Is that so wrong?” He whispered.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Clay is...so broken and so beautiful. That is the only way i can describe him. He is really beautiful person on the inside... Except he has one problem which screwed up his life epically - his parents don't care about him, they never supported him, and he was cast out from their lives leading to his ultimate destruction...Until he moved from Florida to Virginia. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Clay grabbed my hands and placed them over his heart. I could feel the erratic beat beneath my palm. “You ran into my life, this beautiful, amazing girl who changed everything. I finally saw what my world could be. What being normal and happy could look like. You've given me everything I never thought I could have! It scares me to think of life without you. Of not seeing your smile or hearing your voice. (...) And all I could see was my life without you in it. And it was a fucking dark and horrible place.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>He is soooooo broken, he is so unstable, but Maggie shows him that world can be such a fun place, such a beautiful thing and that it can all be well... But can he really battle his inner demons and win? <br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>OTHER CHARACTERS:</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Rachel and Danniel......SADHASJKDAHSDJASH damn them xD (especially Danny), but not in the bad way - they love Maggie and they support her, but they sometimes just irritated me. But i liked them nonetheless. <br>Lisa and Ruby were great, i love them, and i loved how thoughtful are... They are two beautiful women and they are just amazing.<br>Maggie's parents....too overprotective and controlling. But they only want what is best for their daughter and i understood that. But they overreacted many many times...<br>But Clay's parents are another story...They are the worst kind of parents ever, if they can even be called parents. They are great manipulators and their primary weapon is to hurt people with words, and they are quite good at doing it.<br><br><br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>CONCERING THE END: contains serious spoilers</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Oh Clay, he is bipolar and has Borderline Personality Disorder as well...which often leads to manic episodes and a lot of cutting... I couldn't bear reading everytime he did that, and i could only applaud for the courage of Maggie, who stayed with him through it all... She seriously loves him, and he loves her..and even if the stuff seems all doom and gloom, i believe they can make it work!<br>And that letter in the end devastated me T_T Especially after he almost killed himself :( Oh he breaks my heart... :(((((<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And how could they end it that way????????<br>____________________________________________<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>OVERALL</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br>____________________________________________<br><br><br><b> Beautiful, wonderful, captivating, powerful, heartbreaking, devastating, full of awesomeness, full of regrets and "i am sorry", full of laughing, of love and of courage and struggle. I loved every single sentence of it, i loved the story about those two, even though it was sometimes hard to read... But at least i won't have to wait to read the conclusion to this awesome book. <br><br>Thanx Debra for recommending it to me, and check out <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/470330747" rel="nofollow noopener">her wonderful review </a></b> <br><br><b>
  <i>This review can be found on my blog: <a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">infinity-of-time.blogspot.com</a> also known as... </i>
</b><br><a href="http://infinity-of-time.blogspot.com/2013/04/find-you-in-dark-find-you-in-dark-1-by.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380363317i/714576.png" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>____________________________________________<br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br>____________________________________________ <br><br><b>REVIEW(S) RELATED TO THIS BOOK:</b><br><br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/583669536" rel="nofollow noopener"> Find You in the Dark (Find You in the Dark, #1) </a> <br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/583669544" rel="nofollow noopener"> Cloud Walking (Find You in the Dark, #1.5) </a> <br>◈ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/583669553" rel="nofollow noopener"> Light in the Shadows (Find You in the Dark, #2) </a> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="destini mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia"><img alt="destini mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499903277p2/13742215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/585040263?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13742215-destini-mia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer585040263" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10897541309706074440"><i>… everything had started so simply.<br/>A look. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/566287.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>A touch.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/563779.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>A kiss. </i><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399090ra/771948.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Find You In The Dark</i> was <b>raw, beautiful,</b> and <b>soul-moving.</b> I was so emotionally invested that every up and down, every emotion each of the characters expressed, I felt. <br/><br/>Maggie Young has had the closest you can get to a perfect life. <br/>Great friends. Wonderful parents. Good grades.<br/>She has normal. <br/>And then Clayton Reed walks into her life. <br/>They fall into a world of passion and love, where they believe everything will be okay as long as they l</span>
  <span id="freeText10897541309706074440" style="display:none"><i>… everything had started so simply.<br>A look. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/566287.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>A touch.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/563779.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>A kiss. </i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399090ra/771948.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Find You In The Dark</i> was <b>raw, beautiful,</b> and <b>soul-moving.</b> I was so emotionally invested that every up and down, every emotion each of the characters expressed, I felt. <br><br>Maggie Young has had the closest you can get to a perfect life. <br>Great friends. Wonderful parents. Good grades.<br>She has normal. <br>And then Clayton Reed walks into her life. <br>They fall into a world of passion and love, where they believe everything will be okay as long as they loved each other. That together, they can fight off the darkness. <br>But sometimes, love isn’t enough. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416851ra/823767.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> The most perfect memories are the ones too painful to forget.</i><br><br>From the second I started reading, I was hooked. I completely fell in love with the story and the characters. I loved along with them, cried with them, laughed with them. My heart broke for their struggles and for Clay’s illness. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416851ra/823768.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> “You ran into my life, this beautiful, amazing girl who changed everything. I finally saw what my world could be.</i><br><br>One of the things that really stood out for me was the humor. Despite the how heartbreaking and raw their situation was, Maggie and Clay always found a way to make me laugh. <br><br>From the beginning I knew that there was something different about Clay, but it wasn’t so bad that I was <i>really</i> worried. But when Maggie and Clay started falling in love and <b>really</b> getting to know each other, you start to get little clues that tell you that there’s something bigger going on here. <br>And I really admire Maggie because she <b>
  <i>truly</i>
</b> loved Clay. It was utter devotion and unconditional love that she gave this boy, a boy who had never had that. There were times that I believed that maybe their love couldn’t heal him. That maybe it just wasn’t enough. <br><br><i> “As long as we’re together, I have something to fight for.” He whispered. </i><br><br>Maggie was so strong and had such a kind heart. Like anybody, she made mistakes but you could see the good intentions behind them. This was a very delicate situation and she did her best to handle it with care. She hung on when I would have let go. She stuck by his side through the good and the bad. And there was a lot of bad. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416851ra/823769.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b> And maybe what we had, for those few blissful months, had truly been beautiful. Crazy beautiful. Or maybe just crazy.</b>
</i><br><br>I have a lot of mixed feelings towards Clay. When you put all the problems aside, he was so sweet and totally swoon-worthy. You <b>could feel</b> how much he loved Maggie. And it wasn’t some crazy, out of control love. <b>It was true, real, and deep.</b> <br>On the other hand, everything felt so hopeless. There were times when even <i>I</i> would believe in the words he was saying. I wanted so much for everything to work out, for them to get their happily ever after. But I could see how everything was spiraling out of control and how everything was crumbling. <b>I don’t think I’ve ever felt more <i>hopeless</i>. </b> Ever. <br>But despite it all, I fell in love with Clay too.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416851ra/823770.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The ending was <b>devastating.</b> It was going downhill fast and I was just sobbing from how hard it was to read. One thing came after another and it’s a wonder how I survived reading this. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416851ra/823771.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>... if he went into the dark again, this time I would be there to find him– to follow him. </i><br><br>Clay:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379784114i/453748._SY540_.jpg" width="410" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Maggie:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416851i/823772._SY540_.jpg" width="410" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b> The holes would close up. The ripping seams would come together. But I would never be as I was before. Before him. My crazy beautiful love. </b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="10897541309706074440" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_478718628" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/478718628" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/478718628?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=1-2-stars-read">1-2-stars-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478718628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7519019951207321048">My Maggie and Clayton:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402489465i/9944799._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Maggie is opinionated and straightforward 17-years-old teenager with normal life. But when secluded and unpredictable new boy comes to school, her life is about to be completely changed...</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402489465i/9944800.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What started as ordinary teenage romance story, turned into intense and gut-wrenching story of two young people who learnt the hardest way that love and friendship are not always enough to solve real big problems in your life. This story shows us the disastrous consequences of obsessive an</span>
  <span id="freeText7519019951207321048" style="display:none">My Maggie and Clayton:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402489465i/9944799._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Maggie is opinionated and straightforward 17-years-old teenager with normal life. But when secluded and unpredictable new boy comes to school, her life is about to be completely changed...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402489465i/9944800.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What started as ordinary teenage romance story, turned into intense and gut-wrenching story of two young people who learnt the hardest way that love and friendship are not always enough to solve real big problems in your life. This story shows us the disastrous consequences of obsessive and dysfunctional teenage love and believe me, it was not easy to read about.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402489465i/9944801._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have to admit that I really liked author's depiction of teenagers and their thinking. Yes, she may have touched some clichés but otherwise, she managed to describe typical teenage behaviour and feelings to a T.<br><br>However, I struggled with paying 100% attention when reading this book. It just never grabbed me, it never captivated me. I was never living this story together with characters. I read some other books dealing with the same isuess of mental illness and unfortunatelly Find You in the Dark did not reach its potential in my eyes. It was lacking in many ways in my opinion and I simply cannot give it higher rating.<br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/513778719" />
    <a title="Linda ❤️ Sassy, Classy &amp;&amp; a Little Bit of Nasty" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty"><img alt="Linda ❤️ Sassy, Classy &amp;&amp; a Little Bit of Nasty" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1480477020p2/14581722.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/513778719?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Linda ❤️ Sassy, Classy &amp;&amp; a Little Bit of Nasty" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Linda ❤️ Sassy, Classy &amp;&amp; a Little Bit of Nasty" href="/user/show/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty">Linda ❤️ Sassy, Classy &amp;&amp; a Little Bit of Nasty</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,
