              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty?shelf=roller-coaster">roller-coaster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty?shelf=pleasant-surprise">pleasant-surprise</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty?shelf=beautifully-written">beautifully-written</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty?shelf=mature-ya">mature-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty?shelf=troubled-past">troubled-past</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty?shelf=jealousy">jealousy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14581722-linda-sassy-classy-a-little-bit-of-nasty?shelf=female-pov">female-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer513778719" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6632385104570852043"><i>
  <b>Overall Star Rating: 4.5 Stars </b>
</i> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456886771i/18289545._SX540_.png' width='85' height='45' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456886771i/18289545._SX540_.png' width='85' height='45' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456886771i/18289545._SX540_.png' width='85' height='45' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456886771i/18289545._SX540_.png' width='85' height='45' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456890971i/18290085.jpg' width='35' height='45' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Like most books, I didn't read the blurb for this book. I love when it ends up being one of the most self-searching, gut-wrenching books. I had no idea what I was walking into when I started this. The title should have clued me in to <i>something</i>, but I didn't even think to process it. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456887886i/18289704._SX540_.png' width='400' height='30' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Clayton Reed was the new boy in school. He moved from Florida to Virgina and the high school bully thought he found a new chew toy with Clay and after Maggie <i>literally</i> ran int</span>
  <span id="freeText6632385104570852043" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>Overall Star Rating: 4.5 Stars </b>
</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456886771i/18289545._SX540_.png" width="85" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456886771i/18289545._SX540_.png" width="85" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456886771i/18289545._SX540_.png" width="85" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456886771i/18289545._SX540_.png" width="85" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456890971i/18290085.jpg" width="35" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Like most books, I didn't read the blurb for this book. I love when it ends up being one of the most self-searching, gut-wrenching books. I had no idea what I was walking into when I started this. The title should have clued me in to <i>something</i>, but I didn't even think to process it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456887886i/18289704._SX540_.png" width="400" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Clayton Reed was the new boy in school. He moved from Florida to Virgina and the high school bully thought he found a new chew toy with Clay and after Maggie <i>literally</i> ran into Clay earlier that morning, she felt an instant pull to him and felt the need to step in and defend him.<br><br>Maggie bulldozed into Clay's life and she wasn't going to take no as an answer. She wanted to get to know him at all costs, even if he didn't want her to. And he didn't want her to.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456887886i/18289704._SX540_.png" width="400" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Clay is dealing with a very serious mental illness. This illness affected every aspect of his life. It controlled all of his thoughts and <i>reactions.</i> With Clay's dips and rises of his mental illness, Clay and Maggie's budding relationship followed. But even with the dark days, Maggie still saw Clay for Clay, rather than his illness, and she stuck to his side. All through to the bitter end. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456887886i/18289704._SX540_.png" width="400" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maggie came from a very loving family. She was the only child and her parents exuded love. Her parents expressed love for each other openly and showed Maggie that love on a normal basis. <br>Her best friends, Rachel and Daniel, had her back to the ends of the Earth. She had their support and they only had good intentions where Maggie was concerned. Maggie was a strong-willed individual. Kind of difficult not to be, when you knew your support system was pretty solid. <br><br>Maggie Young didn't know what dark was. So the same way she bulldozed into Clay's life, Clay's darkness bulldozed into hers. And for someone who was inexperienced with dark, I felt she handled it pretty well. With that being said, it hurt my heart to see the darkness start to chip away at the person that Maggie was. I saw that the darkness deteriorated Maggie's being and kind of <i>change</i> this strong, courageous person. But even as the darkness ate away at her, she still held Clay's hand. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456889456i/18289872.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>“What is it?" I asked breathlessly. <br>"I love you so much. Sometimes it hurts."<br>"I don't want it to hurt, Clay. Our love should make you feel wonderful.” </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456889517i/18289874.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With Clay's mental illness came the odium of his parents and peers. With Clay's father being a political figure, they didn't want a <i>sick child</i> to taint his image. Clay's mother did everything she could to push him as far out of the picture as she could - the very reason why Clay ended up going to live with his aunt in Virginia.<br><br>Maggie's parents and friends didn't trust Clay. They saw something in him and knew something wasn't right. They didn't know just what, but there was a looming darkness about him to them. They saw the hold that Clay had on Maggie and saw the <i>obsessiveness</i> the two had for each other. Maggie began lying to her parents, and canceling plans with her best friends. Maggie morphed into a different person right before their eyes - and that didn't sit well with them.<br><br>Their relationship almost appeared unhealthy and dysfunctional at times. The tug and pull, the give and take. Some more from one than the other on some days. It was almost difficult to decipher where one heartbeat began and the other's ended, with how <i>fused</i> they were with each other, emotionally. Even with how unhealthy their love appeared, I still couldn't deny that their love was beautiful. It was passionate, forgiving and unyielding. Intense, unrestrained and delicate.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456889456i/18289872.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>“I needed Clay as much as he needed me. We existed in this symbiotic relationship where our hearts beat and our lungs breathed only for each other."</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456889517i/18289874.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With Maggie, Clay saw some semblance of a normal life. He wanted that normal life. He wanted a life where he didn't have to depend on medication. He wanted a life where he could hold a normal conversation without getting angry because the person didn't agree with him. He just wanted to be.......normal.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456889456i/18289872.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>“You ran into my life, this beautiful, amazing girl who changed everything. I finally saw what my world could be. What being normal and happy could look like."</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456889517i/18289874.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book ends with a <b>
  <i>MASSIVE</i>
</b> cliffhanger so have the next books ready. I'd recommend this to someone looking for a deep read who can handle a little beating to their emotions. The feels in this is so intense and definitely opened my eyes immensely. I didn't understand the illness. I won't say I do now, but I've widened my view on it. I was narrow-minded and I didn't allow myself to see what Clay was going through in the beginnings of this book. I judged him off of things he couldn't control as I was reading, and when I got to the end, my whole view on this disease transformed tenfold. Definitely glad I read this book.<br><br>Fair warning, this book holds a lot of:<br><br><i>Jealousy</i><br><i>Ruin</i><br><i>Subjugation (to the illness)</i><br><i>Suffering</i><br><i>Tempers</i><br><i>Distress</i><br><br>Just letting you know, this isn't a light read. So don't go in expecting it to be one. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456887886i/18289704._SX540_.png" width="400" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6632385104570852043" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_515305955" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/515305955" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/515305955?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940015529708" href="/book/show/17303696-find-you-in-the-dark">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=jackass-heroes">jackass-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=drama-rama-bo-bama">drama-rama-bo-bama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=virgin-heroine">virgin-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=heart-breaking">heart-breaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=uber-sweet">uber-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=female-pov">female-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=broken-hero">broken-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=super-steamy">super-steamy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer515305955" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer946566775487998996"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4 Cray-Cray stars ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393267127ra/8684786.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“The most perfect memories are the ones too painful to forget.”<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/>After finishing reading this book, I still don't know what to think. This book was a wild ride. It was some heavy and quite emotional stuff. It touches the subject of mental illness which is never an easy thing to read about. So, let me tell you how this was for me.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393268721i/8685000.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In the very start of the book we meet </span>
  <span id="freeText946566775487998996" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4 Cray-Cray stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393267127ra/8684786.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“The most perfect memories are the ones too painful to forget.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>After finishing reading this book, I still don't know what to think. This book was a wild ride. It was some heavy and quite emotional stuff. It touches the subject of mental illness which is never an easy thing to read about. So, let me tell you how this was for me.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393268721i/8685000.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the very start of the book we meet Maggie Young --the sole narrator of the book--a teenage girl who is laid back, happy, and pretty much speaks her mind. She has her two best friends Rachel and Daniel that love and support her. Then she literally bumps into the "new guy" at her school, Clay Reed. They don't make a very good first impression. But soon, Maggie is determined to become his friend. She finds out Clay has moved in with his aunt after living with his parents in Florida. After, a "problem" they sent him to his aunts.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“When you're in a room, Maggie, all I see is you. You make everything better. Clearer. You stop the crazy noise in my head. I can think, hell, I can breathe when we're together What you make me feel is the most unbelievable and scary thing I've ever felt.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I liked the first part of the book, I really enjoyed it. I was very curious about this hot Clay guy. He seemed so lonely and quiet that I also became intrigued, just like Maggie. I liked seeing them interact, especially with that physical chemistry between them. They were so cute and adorable. But very quickly I realized that there may be something wrong with Clay. His mood swings were giving me whiplash. One moment he was happy and so much fun, the next he would be pissed off and cold. I started to worry about him and wanted to know why he was behaving the way he was.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I love you so much. Sometimes it hurts."<br><br>"I don't want it to hurt, Clay. Our love should make you feel wonderful."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Later on, we find out that there is in fact something wrong with Clay. It becomes hard for Maggie to talk to him because he can spin anything she says to something negative. The more she pushes him in hopes for him to get better, the more difficult it is to be at his side because of how hurtful he can be (no, he did not physically harm her). Clay was stuck in dark place in him mind full of negativity, insecurities, and self loathing. It was so hard for me to read all the harm he caused himself for hope of some sort of relief. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393268689i/8684985._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was so saddened by all of it. I didn't get why no one had ever tried to help Clay, like really help him or monitor his behaviour. The middle to the end, was full of craziness. There was a point where I thought I just couldn't take any more crazy. Things started getting out of control with Clay turing quite cray-cray. I got so frustrated with Maggie, and how quickly she made light of his issues at times. It was obviously serious but she would enable him at times, and that drove me nuts. I get that she was a teen and all that jazz, but she slowly lost herself by becoming completely wrapped in Clay's world. That...I did not like one. Bit.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“And if he went into the dark again, this time I would be there to find him--to follow him. Because I thought, perhaps quite immeasurable that my love could help him. Maybe our love could even do more than just help--maybe it could heal him. Fix him. Fix everything.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I felt for Clay, really I did...but there was a point where I became kind of scared of him. I feared for his safety and that of Maggie's. The whole situation was just messed up. I loved that vulnerable, sweet, and loving side of Clay. Who wouldn't? Especially with the swoony things he would say. But once the dark side came out, he freaked the crap out me. I just wanted him to get the help he so desperately needed.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392706654ra/8598130.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story was well written, but there were parts that it felt like it dragged on a bit. There was some moments of fun, laughter, and a bit of steam. There were some heartbreaking scenes as well. While I enjoyed the first part of the book, I felt like the middle and end frustrated me way too much. All I can say is that the way Clay acted was pretty realistic. This wasn't a rainbows and unicorns kind of story. It was dark and heavy. I wasn't able to completely fall in love with Clay, but I did care for him. I started with liking Maggie, too not liking her too much. She just made so many mistakes. She did end up making the right decision at the very end. It was a sad ending but I thought that it was a perfect for this story. It was just right for both of the main characters. Overall, I thought this was a really good read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="946566775487998996" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/538065596" />
    <a title="K" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16359109-k"><img alt="K" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1357989852p2/16359109.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/538065596?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K" href="/user/show/16359109-k">K</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer538065596" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3808845900316211389"><b>Ƹ̵̡Ӝ̵̨̄Ʒ 5 Ripping My Heart Out Of My Chest Stars! Ƹ̵̡Ӝ̵̨̄Ʒ</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Maybe I was an idiot, or a glutton for punishment. Or maybe I naively subscribed to the foolish notion that my love could save him. Whatever the reason, I entered the room and sank to the carpet beside that sad and broken boy."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409962i/803231._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Because he had, for a moment in time, been my world. My focus, my entire being. And maybe what we had, for those few blissful months, had truly been beautiful. Crazy beautiful. Or maybe just c</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText3808845900316211389" style="display:none"><b>Ƹ̵̡Ӝ̵̨̄Ʒ 5 Ripping My Heart Out Of My Chest Stars! Ƹ̵̡Ӝ̵̨̄Ʒ</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Maybe I was an idiot, or a glutton for punishment. Or maybe I naively subscribed to the foolish notion that my love could save him. Whatever the reason, I entered the room and sank to the carpet beside that sad and broken boy."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409962i/803231._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Because he had, for a moment in time, been my world. My focus, my entire being. And maybe what we had, for those few blissful months, had truly been beautiful. Crazy beautiful. Or maybe just crazy."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>I CAN'T. I JUST CAN'T.</b> I've just finished this story, and I don't know what to do with myself. My emotions are all over the place. I feel like I'm standing on the edge of a cliff and any minute the slightest breeze will push me over the edge. That's pretty much how I felt the entire time I was reading <i>Find You In The Dark</i>. I feel broken... and I've loved every single second of it!<br><br><b>
  <i>Find You In The Dark,</i>
</b>is a beautiful love story abut two 17 year old kids who fall madly and passionately in love. They are each-others worlds. Their love is beautiful, and sometimes downright unhealthy but it made me fall in love with these characters all the more. I <i>felt</i> their love, and I so badly wanted them to get their HEA. Sometimes however, love just isn't enough, no matter much we try to make it be. <br><br><b>Maggie May Young--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409962i/803232._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Goodness is your virtue. Quiet beauty is your weapon."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Maggie May Young</b> is a 17 year old girl living the most normal life you could imagine. She's got good grades, loving parents who still adore each other, and two best friends that she's known since birth. Her life is stable. Boring. That all changes however when she meets, or rather runs into, Clayton Reeds. He's shockingly rude, standoffish, and wants nothing to do with her. Not because of anything she's done, but for his own reasons. He doesn't want to let anyone get close to him. Maggie is very determined to change that. She feels for him. She can sense his loneliness and she wants to be his friend. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The struggle is really hard sometimes. And then I meet you. And I feel stuff that I’ve never felt before. Things that I never thought I would be lucky enough to experience. And I feel so out of control in the way I am with you. Like I’m stripped bare and for once someone sees everything inside of me… the good and the really really ugly.”-Clay</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Clayton Reed--</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This is forever, Maggie. I would follow you into hell if I had to … You are all I want for the rest of my life.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379744471i/89229._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Clayton Reed</b> is, in simple terms, broken. He suffers from mental health issues which causes him to lash out at the ones he loves. He suffers from episodes and suicidal thoughts. He can be downright cold one minute and the next take your breath away with the love you feel for this fictional character. I so wanted to fix Clayton Reed. I ached for him entirely. Clayton Reed and Maggie May Young together was a beautiful thing to read. Though they had many ups and downs, when they were happy it was perfection. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I needed Clay as much as he needed me. We existed in this symbiotic relationship where our hearts beat and our lungs breathed only for each other.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409962i/803233.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"And if he went into the dark again, this time I would be there to find him - to follow him." ~ Maggie</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The entire time I was reading I just knew that something bad was going to happen. I could feel the darkness that would eventually swallow their fragile love. The darkness just waiting for one slip-up, one opening of light to sneak in on...I was right, and I so desperately didn't want to be..<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I knew his love was an intense, hungry thing. I worried for a moment, as I fell asleep, that his love would eat me alive." ~ Maggie</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.~.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When I asked him as to why he only drew the butterflies he had kissed me softly on the mouth. “Because you make me feel free.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409962ra/803234.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>The last few chapters of this book were some of the most heartbreaking that I have EVER read!</b> I knew. In my heart I knew. Things just kept getting worse and worse and I was in denial just like Maggie was. I didn't want to admit that I knew what was going to happen, and even though I knew, I still wasn't prepared for how sad it made me. So incredibly sad. I am so happy that I waited until the sequel was out because I don't know what I would have done without it.<br><br><i>Find You In The Dark</i> was an unforgettable read. It you haven't read it, read it right now! It doesn't matter if this doesn't seem like the type of book for you, you have to give it a shot. It is now earning a spot on my <b>ALL TIME FAVORITES</b> list. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409962ra/803235.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“What I can see so far is that life consists of good and evil, black and white. And everything in between is a struggle for dominating the other. Life is a struggle. And I hate that it all ends with nothingness. That one day, you simply aren't here anymore. No more smiles, no more tears, no more anything.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>*****I would recommend this novel to others*****</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="3808845900316211389" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer13809274035641050456"><br/><b>
  <i>"Sometimes, love can't make everything better, and the best thing for everyone is to walk away. No matter how much it may hurt...."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1360642435p8/691805.jpg' width='300' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>A deeply intense emotional journey....</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/>I<u> LOVED</u> <--------- this book............<br/><br/><br/>This is a heartbreaking love story of two different people who fall in love for the first time only to discover that the reality of the situation is so much darker and bigger than the both of them.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I learned that sometimes <u>“sorry”</u> is not enough......"</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1360642554p8/691806.jpg' width='250' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b> "When I asked him why he</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText13809274035641050456" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>"Sometimes, love can't make everything better, and the best thing for everyone is to walk away. No matter how much it may hurt...."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1360642435p8/691805.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>A deeply intense emotional journey....</b>
</i><br><br><br>I<u> LOVED</u> &lt;--------- this book............<br><br><br>This is a heartbreaking love story of two different people who fall in love for the first time only to discover that the reality of the situation is so much darker and bigger than the both of them.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I learned that sometimes <u>“sorry”</u> is not enough......"</i>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1360642554p8/691806.jpg" width="250" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b> "When I asked him why he only drew the butterflies he had kissed me softly on the mouth - Because you make me feel free". </b>
</i> <br><br><br><br>I absolutely loved this book but it was an extremely emotional read for me. This story is not your typical predictable love story. It was deep, heart wrenching and emotional. While reading the book I felt I was there in the moment seeing, experiencing and feeling everything that was happening between Maggie and Clay - it felt so real. <br><br><i>
  <b>"I had wondered a million times how I could possibly go on living when my heart was gone? How was it possible that it still beat in my chest when it felt so empty?"</b>
</i><br><br><br>It was sad watching Maggie change throughout the book. She started off a strong, determined, happy person and slowly turned into an emotionally scarred and angry girl. I adored Clay - it was so difficult to watch him struggle with who he was and what he truly wanted to be. <br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I knew this was bad for me..... We existed in this symbiotic relationship where our hearts beat and our lungs breathed only for each other".</b>
</i><br><br>The ending <u>killed</u> me! I’m dying to know how Clay and Maggies story *ends* and I can’t wait to get my hands on the *second book next month*!!! <br><br>A <u> highly</u> recommended read!!!!<br><br><br> <b>*****5 Butter flying Stars*****</b><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9619308418839133450">5++++ stars<br/><br/>This book was not at ALL what I was expecting. Totally blew me AWAY! <br/><br/>Maggie is plugging along in her mundane, boring life - just existing. Then she literally runs into Clayton Reed. Everything changes......<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398634i/770635._SY540_.jpg' width='200' height='225' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I love that Maggie was so persistent in pursuing Clay and wasn't afraid to go for it. <br/><br/>I was instantly connected with Maggie.   <span id="freeText9619308418839133450" style="display:none">5++++ stars<br><br>This book was not at ALL what I was expecting. Totally blew me AWAY! <br><br>Maggie is plugging along in her mundane, boring life - just existing. Then she literally runs into Clayton Reed. Everything changes......<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398634i/770635._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I love that Maggie was so persistent in pursuing Clay and wasn't afraid to go for it. <br><br>I was instantly connected with Maggie. I was able to relate to her on many levels. She is trying to hold everything together without anyone knowing something is wrong. She is always having to defend her relationship with Clay and keep her friends and family at arms length to keep them from seeing the truth. Maggie thinks she is protecting Clay, but really she is just enabling him.<br><br>This book was so real and raw. I felt every emotion both Maggie and Clay were experiencing. I related to Maggie's decisions, because at her age, that is exactly what I would have done. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398634i/770636.jpg" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>This is one of the best books I have read this year</b></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1vd04S3z7K+cMOqlW6/gCazQ3bqQcZSuawo9VaCXMiRV4tiScpPLVCkKg8j+aPFbHSrvkv++mVVjJsJeEsWTZA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('eSmkeEeH6W7bBGMQjCXHKHEEkU1fuaZJPCPKzbfBBj/6PAgLGOfOlW4+Cn0p4tZ6wP6jZTB2q7I0DzXGBZOnfw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

    go = function () {
      for (i = 0; i < n; i += 1) {
        script = d.createElement('SCRIPT');
        script.type = 'text/javascript';
        script.async = true;
        script.src = load[i];
        first.parentNode.insertBefore(script, first);
      }
    }
  if (w.attachEvent) {
    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
  }
}(window, document,

    ]
